## ğŸ’° **æ··åˆæ”¯ä»˜ç³»ç»Ÿè®¾è®¡**

### **å¾®ä¿¡æ”¯ä»˜ä¼˜å…ˆ+ä¼ä¸šå¾®ä¿¡ç”Ÿæ€é›†æˆ**

#### **æ ¸å¿ƒè®¾è®¡ç†å¿µï¼šå¾®ä¿¡ç”Ÿæ€æ·±åº¦èåˆ**
```python
# å¾®ä¿¡æ”¯ä»˜+ä¼ä¸šå¾®ä¿¡ä¸€ä½“åŒ–è®¾è®¡
WECHAT_ECOSYSTEM_INTEGRATION = {
    "payment_priority": {
        "primary": "å¾®ä¿¡æ”¯ä»˜ï¼ˆä¼ä¸šç‰ˆï¼‰",
        "secondary": "æ”¯ä»˜å®",
        "tertiary": "é“¶è¡Œè½¬è´¦",
        "crypto": "USDT/USDCï¼ˆWeb3åœºæ™¯ï¼‰"
    },
    "enterprise_wechat_benefits": {
        "real_time_notification": "æ”¶æ¬¾ã€åˆ†è´¦ã€å¼‚å¸¸å®æ—¶æ¨é€",
        "approval_workflow": "å¤§é¢åˆ†è´¦ä¼ä¸šå¾®ä¿¡å®¡æ‰¹",
        "customer_service": "ä¼ä¸šå¾®ä¿¡ç¾¤ç»„å®¢æœæ”¯æŒ",
        "data_dashboard": "ä¼ä¸šå¾®ä¿¡å°ç¨‹åºæŸ¥çœ‹ä¸šåŠ¡æ•°æ®"
    },
    "instant_settlement": {
        "trigger": "æ”¶æ¬¾ç¡®è®¤å30ç§’å†…å®Œæˆåˆ†è´¦",
        "safety_margin": "å¹³å°ç•™å­˜15%ä½œä¸ºé£é™©ç¼“å†²",
        "notification": "åˆ†è´¦å®Œæˆä¼ä¸šå¾®ä¿¡ç«‹å³é€šçŸ¥å„æ–¹"
    }
}
```

#### **å®æ—¶åˆ†è´¦æŠ€æœ¯å®ç°**
```python
# å®æ—¶åˆ†è´¦ç³»ç»Ÿ - å¾®ä¿¡æ”¯ä»˜ä¼˜å…ˆè®¾è®¡
class WeChatRealTimeSettlement:
    def __init__(self):
        self.wechat_pay_api = WeChatPayAPI()
        self.enterprise_wechat_api = EnterpriseWeChatAPI()
        self.safety_margin = 0.15  # 15%å®‰å…¨è¾¹é™…
    
    def process_instant_settlement(self, payment_record):
        """
        æ”¶æ¬¾å30ç§’å†…å®æ—¶åˆ†è´¦ - å¾®ä¿¡ç”Ÿæ€ä¼˜åŠ¿
        """
        try:
            # 1. æ”¶æ¬¾ç¡®è®¤ï¼ˆå¾®ä¿¡æ”¯ä»˜å›è°ƒï¼‰
            if payment_record.payment_method == "wechat_pay":
                confirmation = self.wechat_pay_api.verify_payment(payment_record)
                if not confirmation.success:
                    return {"status": "pending", "reason": "payment_not_confirmed"}
            
            # 2. è®¡ç®—åˆ†è´¦é‡‘é¢ï¼ˆä¿ç•™å®‰å…¨è¾¹é™…ï¼‰
            total_amount = payment_record.amount
            splits = self.calculate_safe_splits(payment_record.case_id, total_amount)
            
            # 3. æ‰§è¡Œå®æ—¶åˆ†è´¦
            settlement_results = []
            
            # æœºæ„åˆ†è´¦ï¼ˆå¾®ä¿¡ä¼ä¸šè½¬è´¦ï¼‰
            institution_result = self.wechat_pay_api.transfer_to_enterprise(
                amount=splits["institution_amount"],
                account=get_institution_wechat_account(payment_record.case_id),
                description=f"æ¡ˆä»¶{payment_record.case_id}æœºæ„åˆ†æˆ"
            )
            settlement_results.append(("institution", institution_result))
            
            # å¾‹å¸ˆåˆ†è´¦ï¼ˆå¾®ä¿¡ä¸ªäººè½¬è´¦ï¼‰
            lawyer_result = self.wechat_pay_api.transfer_to_personal(
                amount=splits["lawyer_amount"],
                account=get_lawyer_wechat_account(payment_record.case_id),
                description=f"æ¡ˆä»¶{payment_record.case_id}å¾‹å¸ˆä½£é‡‘"
            )
            settlement_results.append(("lawyer", lawyer_result))
            
            # é”€å”®åˆ†è´¦ï¼ˆå¾®ä¿¡ä¸ªäººè½¬è´¦ï¼‰
            sales_result = self.wechat_pay_api.transfer_to_personal(
                amount=splits["sales_amount"],
                account=get_sales_wechat_account(payment_record.case_id),
                description=f"æ¡ˆä»¶{payment_record.case_id}é”€å”®ä½£é‡‘"
            )
            settlement_results.append(("sales", sales_result))
            
            # 4. ä¼ä¸šå¾®ä¿¡å®æ—¶é€šçŸ¥
            self.send_enterprise_wechat_notifications(payment_record, splits, settlement_results)
            
            # 5. å¹³å°ç•™å­˜ï¼ˆå®‰å…¨è¾¹é™…+å‡€åˆ©æ¶¦ï¼‰
            platform_retained = splits["platform_amount"] + splits["safety_margin"]
            
            return {
                "status": "completed",
                "settlement_time": "30ç§’",
                "total_distributed": sum([s["amount"] for _, s in settlement_results if s["success"]]),
                "platform_retained": platform_retained,
                "notification_sent": True
            }
            
        except Exception as e:
            # åˆ†è´¦å¤±è´¥ï¼Œä¼ä¸šå¾®ä¿¡å‘Šè­¦
            self.enterprise_wechat_api.send_alert_message(
                message=f"âš ï¸ åˆ†è´¦å¤±è´¥ï¼šæ¡ˆä»¶{payment_record.case_id}ï¼Œé”™è¯¯ï¼š{str(e)}",
                users=["admin_user_id"]
            )
            return {"status": "failed", "error": str(e)}
    
    def calculate_safe_splits(self, case_id, total_amount):
        """
        è®¡ç®—å®‰å…¨åˆ†è´¦ - é‡‡ç”¨åŒå±‚æ¨¡å‹å¹¶ä¿ç•™é£é™©ç¼“å†²
        """
        # åŸºç¡€åˆ†è´¦æ¯”ä¾‹ï¼ˆåŸºäºæœåŠ¡åˆ†æˆæ± ï¼‰
        base_splits_in_pool = {
            "lawyer_rate": 0.20,         # å¾‹å¸ˆå æœåŠ¡æ± 20%
            "sales_rate": 0.15,          # é”€å”®å æœåŠ¡æ± 15%
            "platform_rate": 0.65        # å¹³å°å æœåŠ¡æ± 65%
        }
        institution_return_rate = 0.50   # æœºæ„å›ºå®šè¿”è¿˜50%

        # å‡å»å®‰å…¨è¾¹é™…åçš„å¯åˆ†é…æ€»é¢
        distributable_amount = total_amount * (1 - self.safety_margin)
        
        # åœ¨å¯åˆ†é…æ€»é¢ä¸­è®¡ç®—å„æ–¹å®é™…é‡‘é¢
        institution_amount = distributable_amount * institution_return_rate
        service_pool_amount = distributable_amount * (1 - institution_return_rate)

        lawyer_amount = service_pool_amount * base_splits_in_pool["lawyer_rate"]
        sales_amount = service_pool_amount * base_splits_in_pool["sales_rate"]
        platform_amount = service_pool_amount * base_splits_in_pool["platform_rate"]

        return {
            "institution_amount": institution_amount,
            "platform_amount": platform_amount,
            "lawyer_amount": lawyer_amount,
            "sales_amount": sales_amount,
            "safety_margin": total_amount * self.safety_margin
        }
    
    def send_enterprise_wechat_notifications(self, payment_record, splits, results):
        """
        ä¼ä¸šå¾®ä¿¡å®æ—¶é€šçŸ¥æ¨é€
        """
        # ç»™æœºæ„æ¨é€
        institution_message = f"""
        ğŸ’° æ”¶æ¬¾é€šçŸ¥
        æ¡ˆä»¶ç¼–å·ï¼š{payment_record.case_id}
        æ”¶æ¬¾é‡‘é¢ï¼šÂ¥{payment_record.amount:,.2f}
        æ‚¨çš„åˆ†æˆï¼šÂ¥{splits['institution_amount']:,.2f}
        åˆ°è´¦çŠ¶æ€ï¼š{'âœ… å·²åˆ°è´¦' if results[0][1]['success'] else 'âŒ å¤„ç†ä¸­'}
        åˆ°è´¦æ—¶é—´ï¼š{datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')}
        """
        
        self.enterprise_wechat_api.send_message(
            user_id=get_institution_contact(payment_record.case_id),
            message=institution_message
        )
        
        # ç»™å¾‹å¸ˆæ¨é€
        lawyer_message = f"""
        ğŸ’¸ ä½£é‡‘åˆ°è´¦é€šçŸ¥
        æ¡ˆä»¶ç¼–å·ï¼š{payment_record.case_id}
        æ‚¨çš„ä½£é‡‘ï¼šÂ¥{splits['lawyer_amount']:,.2f}
        åˆ°è´¦çŠ¶æ€ï¼š{'âœ… å·²åˆ°è´¦' if results[1][1]['success'] else 'âŒ å¤„ç†ä¸­'}
        """
        
        self.enterprise_wechat_api.send_message(
            user_id=get_lawyer_contact(payment_record.case_id),
            message=lawyer_message
        )
```

# å…è´¹éƒ¨ç½²é£æ§ç³»ç»Ÿ
class FreeDeploymentRiskControl:
    def __init__(self):
        self.evaluation_criteria = {
            "financial_score": 40,    # è´¢åŠ¡å®åŠ›40%
            "business_score": 30,     # ä¸šåŠ¡è§„æ¨¡30%
            "reputation_score": 20,   # è¡Œä¸šå£°èª‰20%
            "cooperation_score": 10   # åˆä½œæ„æ„¿10%
        }
    
    def evaluate_client_qualification(self, client_info):
        """
        å®¢æˆ·èµ„æ ¼è¯„ä¼° - å†³å®šæ˜¯å¦æä¾›å…è´¹éƒ¨ç½²
        """
        scores = {
            "financial": self.evaluate_financial_strength(client_info),
            "business": self.evaluate_business_scale(client_info),
            "reputation": self.evaluate_market_reputation(client_info),
            "cooperation": self.evaluate_cooperation_intention(client_info)
        }
        
        total_score = (
            scores["financial"] * 0.4 +
            scores["business"] * 0.3 +
            scores["reputation"] * 0.2 +
            scores["cooperation"] * 0.1
        )
        
        if total_score >= 85:
            return {
                "qualified": True,
                "tier": "premium",
                "commission_rate": 0.15,
                "deployment_cost": 0,
                "guarantee_required": 1000000  # 100ä¸‡ä¿è¯é‡‘
            }
        elif total_score >= 75:
            return {
                "qualified": True,
                "tier": "standard", 
                "commission_rate": 0.2,
                "deployment_cost": 0,
                "guarantee_required": 2000000  # 200ä¸‡ä¿è¯é‡‘
            }
        else:
            return {
                "qualified": False,
                "reason": "è´¢åŠ¡å®åŠ›æˆ–ä¸šåŠ¡è§„æ¨¡ä¸ç¬¦åˆå…è´¹éƒ¨ç½²æ¡ä»¶",
                "alternative": "å»ºè®®é€‰æ‹©ä»˜è´¹éƒ¨ç½²æ–¹æ¡ˆ"
            }
    
    def setup_commission_monitoring(self, client_id, commission_rate):
        """
        ä½£é‡‘ç›‘æ§ç³»ç»Ÿ - ç¡®ä¿æŒ‰æ—¶æ”¶å–
        """
        monitoring_config = {
            "auto_calculation": True,           # è‡ªåŠ¨è®¡ç®—ä½£é‡‘
            "real_time_tracking": True,         # å®æ—¶è¿½è¸ªä¸šåŠ¡æµæ°´
            "monthly_settlement": True,         # æœˆåº¦ç»“ç®—
            "early_warning": {
                "payment_delay": 7,             # 7å¤©æœªä»˜æ¬¾é¢„è­¦
                "volume_decline": 0.3,          # ä¸šåŠ¡é‡ä¸‹é™30%é¢„è­¦
                "credit_degradation": True      # ä¿¡ç”¨è¯„çº§ä¸‹é™é¢„è­¦
            },
            "penalty_mechanism": {
                "late_payment_fee": 0.05,       # é€¾æœŸè´¹ç‡5%/æœˆ
                "service_suspension": 30,       # 30å¤©æœªä»˜æ¬¾æš‚åœæœåŠ¡
                "legal_action": 90              # 90å¤©æœªä»˜æ¬¾æ³•å¾‹è¿½å¿
            }
        }
        
        return self.deploy_monitoring_system(client_id, monitoring_config)
```

### **é€šç”¨åŒ–é…ç½®å¼•æ“**

# ä¸šåŠ¡æµç¨‹é…ç½®å¼•æ“ - åå°å¯è§†åŒ–é…ç½®
class BusinessProcessConfigurator:
    def configure_workflow(self, tenant_id, scenario_type):
        """
        å¯è§†åŒ–é…ç½®ä¸šåŠ¡æµç¨‹ - æ‹–æ‹½å¼æµç¨‹è®¾è®¡
        """
        workflow_templates = {
            "legal_collection": [
                {"step": "case_assignment", "configurable": True},
                {"step": "document_generation", "ai_enabled": True},
                {"step": "communication_sequence", "multichannel": True},
                {"step": "payment_tracking", "split_rules": "configurable"},
                {"step": "completion_verification", "auto_manual": "both"}
            ],
            "web3_development": [
                {"step": "requirement_analysis", "ai_assisted": True},
                {"step": "developer_matching", "skill_based": True},
                {"step": "milestone_planning", "smart_contracts": True},
                {"step": "code_review", "automated": True},
                {"step": "payment_release", "escrow_based": True}
            ]
        }
        
        return self.customize_workflow(workflow_templates[scenario_type], tenant_id)
```

### **é€šç”¨åŒ–æ•°æ®åº“è®¾è®¡**

#### **å¤šç§Ÿæˆ·ç®¡ç†è¡¨**
```sql
-- ç§Ÿæˆ·ç®¡ç†è¡¨ï¼ˆæ ¸å¿ƒï¼šæ”¯æŒSaaSå’Œç‹¬ç«‹éƒ¨ç½²ä¸¤ç§æ¨¡å¼ï¼‰
CREATE TABLE tenants (
    id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    tenant_code VARCHAR(50) UNIQUE,
    company_name VARCHAR(200),
    deployment_type ENUM('saas', 'on_premise'), -- SaaSåœ¨çº¿ or æ‰“åŒ…éƒ¨ç½²
    subscription_plan VARCHAR(50), -- è®¢é˜…è®¡åˆ’
    custom_domain VARCHAR(100),    -- è‡ªå®šä¹‰åŸŸå
    feature_flags JSONB,           -- åŠŸèƒ½å¼€å…³é…ç½®
    system_config JSONB,           -- ç³»ç»Ÿé…ç½®
    api_limits JSONB,              -- APIä½¿ç”¨é™åˆ¶
    billing_info JSONB,            -- è®¡è´¹ä¿¡æ¯
    status ENUM('active', 'suspended', 'trial') DEFAULT 'trial',
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW(),
    updated_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW()
);

-- ä¸šåŠ¡åœºæ™¯é…ç½®è¡¨ï¼ˆæ ¸å¿ƒï¼šé€šç”¨åŒ–ä¸šåŠ¡æµç¨‹é…ç½®ï¼‰
CREATE TABLE business_scenarios (
    id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    tenant_id INTEGER REFERENCES tenants(id),
    scenario_code VARCHAR(50), -- 'legal_collection', 'web3_dev', 'content_creation'
    scenario_name VARCHAR(100),
    workflow_config JSONB,     -- å·¥ä½œæµé…ç½®
    role_config JSONB,         -- è§’è‰²é…ç½®
    kpi_config JSONB,          -- KPIé…ç½®
    commission_rules JSONB,    -- åˆ†æˆè§„åˆ™é…ç½®
    automation_rules JSONB,    -- è‡ªåŠ¨åŒ–è§„åˆ™
    is_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT TRUE,
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW(),
    updated_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW(),
    UNIQUE(tenant_id, scenario_code)
);

-- å‚æ•°é…ç½®è¡¨ï¼ˆæ ¸å¿ƒï¼šæ‰€æœ‰å¯è°ƒå‚æ•°éƒ½åœ¨è¿™é‡Œï¼‰
CREATE TABLE system_parameters (
    id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    tenant_id INTEGER REFERENCES tenants(id),
    scenario_id INTEGER REFERENCES business_scenarios(id),
    category VARCHAR(50), -- 'quotas', 'thresholds', 'rates', 'limits'
    param_key VARCHAR(100),
    param_value JSONB,
    param_type VARCHAR(20), -- 'number', 'percentage', 'json', 'boolean'
    description TEXT,
    min_value DECIMAL,
    max_value DECIMAL,
    editable BOOLEAN DEFAULT TRUE,
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW(),
    updated_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW(),
    UNIQUE(tenant_id, scenario_id, category, param_key)
);

-- ç”¨æˆ·è¡¨ï¼ˆä¼˜åŒ–ï¼šå¤šç§Ÿæˆ·æ”¯æŒï¼‰
CREATE TABLE users (
    id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    tenant_id INTEGER REFERENCES tenants(id),
    username VARCHAR(50),
    password_hash VARCHAR(255),
    phone VARCHAR(20),
    email VARCHAR(100),
    real_name VARCHAR(50),
    user_role VARCHAR(50), -- å¯é…ç½®è§’è‰²ï¼Œä¸å†å›ºå®šæšä¸¾
    permissions JSONB,     -- åŠ¨æ€æƒé™é…ç½®
    department VARCHAR(100),
    manager_id INTEGER REFERENCES users(id),
    status ENUM('active', 'inactive', 'banned') DEFAULT 'active',
    last_login TIMESTAMP,
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW(),
    updated_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW(),
    UNIQUE(tenant_id, username),
    UNIQUE(tenant_id, phone)
);

-- ä¸šåŠ¡å®ä½“è¡¨ï¼ˆé€šç”¨ï¼šæ”¯æŒå„ç§ä¸šåŠ¡å¯¹è±¡ï¼‰
CREATE TABLE business_entities (
    id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    tenant_id INTEGER REFERENCES tenants(id),
    scenario_id INTEGER REFERENCES business_scenarios(id),
    entity_type VARCHAR(50), -- 'case', 'project', 'task', 'order'
    entity_code VARCHAR(100),
    title VARCHAR(200),
    description TEXT,
    status VARCHAR(50),
    priority_level INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    assigned_to INTEGER REFERENCES users(id),
    created_by INTEGER REFERENCES users(id),
    business_data JSONB,   -- çµæ´»å­˜å‚¨å„ç§ä¸šåŠ¡æ•°æ®
    workflow_state JSONB, -- å·¥ä½œæµçŠ¶æ€
    kpi_metrics JSONB,    -- KPIæŒ‡æ ‡æ•°æ®
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW(),
    updated_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW(),
    INDEX(tenant_id, scenario_id, entity_type),
    INDEX(tenant_id, assigned_to, status)
);

-- è´¢åŠ¡è®°å½•è¡¨ï¼ˆé€šç”¨ï¼šæ”¯æŒå„ç§æ”¶ä»˜æ¬¾åœºæ™¯ï¼‰
CREATE TABLE financial_records (
    id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    tenant_id INTEGER REFERENCES tenants(id),
    entity_id INTEGER REFERENCES business_entities(id),
    record_type ENUM('income', 'expense', 'commission', 'refund'),
    amount DECIMAL(15,2),
    currency VARCHAR(10) DEFAULT 'CNY',
    payment_method VARCHAR(50),
    payment_channel VARCHAR(50),
    transaction_id VARCHAR(100),
    payer_info JSONB,
    payee_info JSONB,
    split_rules JSONB,     -- åˆ†è´¦è§„åˆ™
    split_status ENUM('pending', 'processing', 'completed', 'failed'),
    fees JSONB,           -- æ‰‹ç»­è´¹ä¿¡æ¯
    status ENUM('pending', 'confirmed', 'cancelled') DEFAULT 'pending',
    processed_at TIMESTAMP,
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW()
);

-- é…ç½®å˜æ›´æ—¥å¿—è¡¨ï¼ˆé‡è¦ï¼šé…ç½®ä¿®æ”¹è¿½è¸ªï¼‰
CREATE TABLE config_change_logs (
    id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    tenant_id INTEGER REFERENCES tenants(id),
    changed_by INTEGER REFERENCES users(id),
    table_name VARCHAR(50),
    record_id INTEGER,
    field_name VARCHAR(50),
    old_value JSONB,
    new_value JSONB,
    change_reason TEXT,
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW(),
    INDEX(tenant_id, table_name, record_id)
);
```

### **æ•°æ®å¯è§æ€§ä¸å±•ç¤ºé€»è¾‘ (æ ¸å¿ƒè®¾è®¡)**

ä¸ºå®ç°å¯¹å¤–æ¿€åŠ±ä¸å¯¹å†…æˆæœ¬æ§åˆ¶çš„å¹³è¡¡ï¼Œç³»ç»Ÿé‡‡ç”¨åŒå±‚æ•°æ®å±•ç¤ºé€»è¾‘ã€‚æ­¤è®¾è®¡ä¸ºå¹³å°æ ¸å¿ƒå•†ä¸šç­–ç•¥ï¼Œå¼€å‘æ—¶å¿…é¡»ä¸¥æ ¼éµå®ˆã€‚

**1. ä¸¤å¤§æ ¸å¿ƒé‡‘é¢æ¦‚å¿µå®šä¹‰**

-   **æ€»å›æ¬¾é‡‘é¢ (Total Collected Amount)**: å€ºåŠ¡äººå®é™…æ”¯ä»˜çš„å…¨éƒ¨æ¬¾é¡¹ï¼Œæ˜¯æ‰€æœ‰è®¡ç®—çš„æœ€é«˜å±‚çº§çš„åŸºæ•°ã€‚**æ­¤æ•°æ®ä»…å¯¹å¹³å°ç®¡ç†å‘˜å¯è§**ã€‚
-   **æœåŠ¡åˆ†æˆæ±  (Service Pool)**: æ€»å›æ¬¾é‡‘é¢æ‰£é™¤è¿”è¿˜ç»™é‡‘èæœºæ„çš„50%åï¼Œå‰©ä½™çš„å¯ä¾›å¹³å°ã€å¾‹å¸ˆã€é”€å”®ä¸‰æ–¹åˆ†é…çš„é‡‘é¢ã€‚è®¡ç®—å…¬å¼ä¸ºï¼š`æœåŠ¡åˆ†æˆæ±  = æ€»å›æ¬¾é‡‘é¢ * 50%`ã€‚

**2. è§’è‰²æ•°æ®è®¿é—®æƒé™**

-   **å¾‹å¸ˆ (Lawyer) & é”€å”® (Sales)**:
    -   **ç»å¯¹éš”ç¦»**: åœ¨ä»–ä»¬çš„æ‰€æœ‰ç•Œé¢ï¼ŒåŒ…æ‹¬ä¸ªäººä¸­å¿ƒã€ä»ªè¡¨æ¿ã€ä¸šç»©æŠ¥è¡¨ã€ç»“ç®—å•ç­‰ï¼Œ**ç»å¯¹ä¸èƒ½**å‡ºç°â€œæ€»å›æ¬¾é‡‘é¢â€ã€‚
    -   **å”¯ä¸€åŸºæ•°**: æ‰€æœ‰ä¸ä»–ä»¬ç›¸å…³çš„â€œæ€»é‡‘é¢â€ã€â€œä¸šç»©åŸºæ•°â€ç­‰ï¼Œ**å¿…é¡»**æ˜¯â€œæœåŠ¡åˆ†æˆæ± â€çš„é‡‘é¢ã€‚
    -   **å±•ç¤ºæ¯”ä¾‹**: ä»–ä»¬çœ‹åˆ°çš„ä½£é‡‘æ¯”ä¾‹æ˜¯åŸºäºâ€œæœåŠ¡åˆ†æˆæ± â€è®¡ç®—çš„ï¼ˆå¾‹å¸ˆ20%ï¼Œé”€å”®15%ï¼‰ã€‚

-   **å¹³å°ç®¡ç†å‘˜ (Admin)**:
    -   **å®Œå…¨å¯è§**: æ‹¥æœ‰æœ€é«˜æƒé™ï¼Œå¯ä»¥çœ‹åˆ°ä»â€œæ€»å›æ¬¾é‡‘é¢â€åˆ°å„æ–¹æœ€ç»ˆåˆ†æˆçš„å®Œæ•´èµ„é‡‘é“¾è·¯å’ŒçœŸå®æ•°æ®ã€‚

**3. åç«¯å®ç°ä¼ªä»£ç ç¤ºä¾‹**

```python
# æ•°æ®æŸ¥è¯¢å±‚çš„æƒé™æ§åˆ¶
def get_performance_data(user_id, role):
    """
    æ ¹æ®ç”¨æˆ·è§’è‰²è¿”å›ä¸åŒçš„ä¸šç»©æ•°æ®è§†å›¾
    """
    if role in ['lawyer', 'sales']:
        # å¯¹äºå¾‹å¸ˆå’Œé”€å”®ï¼Œä»â€œæœåŠ¡åˆ†æˆæ± â€è§†å›¾ä¸­æŸ¥è¯¢æ•°æ®
        # SQLæŸ¥è¯¢ç¤ºä¾‹: SELECT ... FROM V_SERVICE_POOL_PERFORMANCE WHERE user_id = ...
        data = query_from_service_pool_view(user_id)
        
        # è¿”å›çš„æ•°æ®ä¸åŒ…å«æ€»å›æ¬¾é¢
        # ä¾‹å¦‚: data['total_base_amount'] æ˜¯æœåŠ¡åˆ†æˆæ± çš„é‡‘é¢
        return {
            "display_commission_rate": "20%" if role == 'lawyer' else "15%",
            "performance_base_amount": data.service_pool_total, # ä¸šç»©åŸºæ•°æ˜¯æœåŠ¡æ± é‡‘é¢
            "calculated_commission": data.commission_amount
        }
        
    elif role == 'admin':
        # ç®¡ç†å‘˜ä»åŒ…å«æ‰€æœ‰çœŸå®æ•°æ®çš„è§†å›¾ä¸­æŸ¥è¯¢
        # SQLæŸ¥è¯¢ç¤ºä¾‹: SELECT ... FROM V_FULL_FINANCIALS WHERE ...
        data = query_from_full_financial_view()
        
        return {
            "total_collected_amount": data.total_collected,
            "institution_return": data.institution_amount,
            "service_pool_amount": data.service_pool,
            "platform_share": data.platform_amount,
            "lawyer_share": data.lawyer_amount,
            "sales_share": data.sales_amount
        }
    else:
        raise PermissionError("æ— æƒè®¿é—®æ•°æ®")

```

### **é…ç½®å®æ—¶ç”Ÿæ•ˆæœºåˆ¶**
```python
# é…ç½®çƒ­æ›´æ–°ç³»ç»Ÿ
class ConfigurationManager:
    def __init__(self):
        self.config_cache = {}
        self.update_listeners = []
    
    def update_parameter(self, tenant_id, param_key, new_value, changed_by):
        """
        æ›´æ–°å‚æ•°é…ç½®å¹¶å®æ—¶ç”Ÿæ•ˆ
        """
        old_value = self.get_parameter(tenant_id, param_key)
        
        # ä¿å­˜æ–°é…ç½®
        self.save_parameter_change(tenant_id, param_key, new_value, changed_by)
        
        # è®°å½•å˜æ›´æ—¥å¿—
        self.log_config_change(tenant_id, param_key, old_value, new_value, changed_by)
        
        # æ›´æ–°ç¼“å­˜
        self.config_cache[f"{tenant_id}:{param_key}"] = new_value
        
        # é€šçŸ¥æ‰€æœ‰ç›‘å¬è€…
        self.notify_config_change(tenant_id, param_key, new_value)
        
        # è§¦å‘ç›¸å…³ä¸šåŠ¡é€»è¾‘æ›´æ–°
        self.apply_config_change(tenant_id, param_key, new_value)
    
    def apply_config_change(self, tenant_id, param_key, new_value):
        """
        åº”ç”¨é…ç½®å˜æ›´åˆ°ä¸šåŠ¡é€»è¾‘
        """
        change_handlers = {
            "daily_sms_quota": self.update_sms_quota_limits,
            "commission_rates": self.recalculate_pending_commissions,
            "kpi_thresholds": self.refresh_performance_evaluations,
            "workflow_steps": self.update_active_workflows
        }
        
        if param_key in change_handlers:
            change_handlers[param_key](tenant_id, new_value)
```

### å…³é”®æŠ€æœ¯å®ç°

#### **APIèµ„æºæ± ç»Ÿä¸€ç®¡ç†ç³»ç»Ÿ**
```python
class APIResourceManager:
    """APIèµ„æºæ± ç®¡ç†å™¨"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.sms_providers = ['é˜¿é‡Œäº‘', 'è…¾è®¯äº‘', 'åä¸ºäº‘', 'å®¹è”äº‘']
        self.voice_providers = ['è®¯é£è¯­éŸ³', 'ç™¾åº¦AI', 'è…¾è®¯äº‘']
        self.payment_providers = ['å¾®ä¿¡æ”¯ä»˜', 'æ”¯ä»˜å®', 'é“¶è”', 'Polygon']
        
    def get_best_sms_provider(self, volume, target_region):
        """æ™ºèƒ½é€‰æ‹©æœ€ä¼˜çŸ­ä¿¡ä¾›åº”å•†"""
        # æ ¹æ®å‘é€é‡ã€åœ°åŒºã€ä»·æ ¼è‡ªåŠ¨é€‰æ‹©
        return self.auto_select_provider('sms', volume, target_region)
        
    def fallback_mechanism(self, primary_failed, service_type):
        """APIæ•…éšœè‡ªåŠ¨åˆ‡æ¢"""
        # ä¸»APIå¤±è´¥æ—¶è‡ªåŠ¨åˆ‡æ¢å¤‡ç”¨API
        pass
```

        "cost": "Â¥0.05/æ¡",

    }

# æˆæœ¬æ§åˆ¶æœºåˆ¶
def send_sms_with_control(phone, content, case_id):
    # 1. æ£€æŸ¥æ—¥å‘é€é™é¢ (500æ¡/å¤©)
    if get_daily_sms_count() >= 500:
        return {"status": "quota_exceeded", "suggest": "manual_call"}
    
    # 2. å»é‡æ£€æŸ¥ (åŒä¸€æ¡ˆä»¶24å°æ—¶å†…æœ€å¤š3æ¡)

#### **2. é‚®ä»¶å‘é€ï¼ˆä½æˆæœ¬æ–¹æ¡ˆï¼‰**

#### **4. AIæœåŠ¡ï¼ˆæŒ‰éœ€ä»˜è´¹ï¼‰**
```python
# é™åˆ¶AIè°ƒç”¨ï¼Œæ§åˆ¶æˆæœ¬
AI_BUDGET_CONTROL = {
    "gpt4_calls_per_day": 100,    # Â¥20/å¤©æˆæœ¬
    "document_generation_limit": 50,  # æ¯æ—¥æ–‡æ¡£ç”Ÿæˆé™åˆ¶
    "cost_alert_threshold": 200   # æœˆæˆæœ¬è­¦å‘Šçº¿
}

def generate_legal_document_with_ai(case_info, document_type):
    # æˆæœ¬æ£€æŸ¥
    if get_monthly_ai_cost() > AI_BUDGET_CONTROL["cost_alert_threshold"]:
        return use_template_fallback(case_info, document_type)
    
    # AIç”Ÿæˆ
    prompt = f"""
    ç”Ÿæˆ{document_type}ï¼Œæ¡ˆä»¶ä¿¡æ¯ï¼š
    å€ºåŠ¡äººï¼š{case_info.debtor_name}
    é‡‘é¢ï¼šÂ¥{case_info.current_amount}
    é€¾æœŸï¼š{case_info.overdue_days}å¤©
    """
    
    response = openai.chat.completions.create(
        model="gpt-4o-mini",  # ä½¿ç”¨æ›´ä¾¿å®œçš„æ¨¡å‹
        messages=[{"role": "user", "content": prompt}],
        max_tokens=1000
    )
    
    # è®°å½•æˆæœ¬
    log_ai_cost(0.2)  # çº¦Â¥0.2/æ¬¡
    
    return response.choices[0].message.content
```

### **Phase 3: å…è´¹/åŠæ‰‹å·¥æ›¿ä»£æ–¹æ¡ˆ**

#### **6. é€šè¯è®°å½•ï¼ˆç®€åŒ–æ–¹æ¡ˆï¼‰**

    "tool": "ä¼ä¸šå¾®ä¿¡/é’‰é’‰",     # å…è´¹å·¥å…·
    "backup": "å½•éŸ³ç¬” + è½¬æ–‡å­—",  # ä½æˆæœ¬ç¡¬ä»¶
    "cost": "Â¥0/æœˆ"

def log_call_manually(case_id, lawyer_id, duration, outcome):

        "case_id": case_id,
        "lawyer_id": lawyer_id,
        "call_time": datetime.now(),

### **APIæˆæœ¬é¢„ç®—æ§åˆ¶**
```python
# æ¯æœˆAPIæˆæœ¬é¢„ç®—
MONTHLY_API_BUDGET = {
    "sms": 500,      # Â¥500 (1ä¸‡æ¡çŸ­ä¿¡)
    "ai": 200,       # Â¥200 (AIæ–‡æ¡£ç”Ÿæˆ) 
    "payment": 100,  # Â¥100 (æ”¯ä»˜æ‰‹ç»­è´¹)
    "email": 0,      # Â¥0 (ä¼ä¸šé‚®ç®±å…è´¹)
    "total": 800     # Â¥800/æœˆæ€»é¢„ç®—
}

# å®æ—¶æˆæœ¬ç›‘æ§
def check_api_budget_status():
    current_usage = get_monthly_api_costs()
    for service, budget in MONTHLY_API_BUDGET.items():
        usage_rate = current_usage[service] / budget
        if usage_rate > 0.8:  # è¶…è¿‡80%é¢„è­¦
            send_budget_alert(service, usage_rate)
        if usage_rate > 1.0:  # è¶…é¢„ç®—åœç”¨
            disable_api_service(service)
```

## ğŸ’³ **å¹³å°ä»£æ”¶ç»Ÿä¸€åˆ†è´¦è¯¦ç»†å®ç°è·¯å¾„**

### **Phase 1: æ”¶æ¬¾ç¯èŠ‚ï¼ˆæŠ€æœ¯å®ç°ï¼‰**

        "method": "dynamic_qr",        # åŠ¨æ€äºŒç»´ç 
        "cost": "0.6%",               # å¾®ä¿¡æ‰‹ç»­è´¹

        "auto_callback": True          # è‡ªåŠ¨å›è°ƒç¡®è®¤
    },

        "cost": "0.55%", 
        "real_time": True,
        "auto_callback": True
    },
    "bank_transfer": {
        "method": "dedicated_account",  # ä¸“ç”¨æ”¶æ¬¾è´¦æˆ·
        "cost": "2-5å…ƒ/ç¬”",           # å›ºå®šæ‰‹ç»­è´¹

        "manual_confirm": True         # äººå·¥ç¡®è®¤
    }
}

# æ”¶æ¬¾å®ç° - ç®€åŒ–ç‰ˆæœ¬ï¼Œé¿å…å¤æ‚API
def create_payment_order(case_id, amount, debtor_info):
    """
    åˆ›å»ºæ”¶æ¬¾è®¢å• - é‡ç‚¹æ˜¯ç®€å•å¯é 
    """
    order = {
        "order_id": f"PAY{case_id}_{int(time.time())}",
        "case_id": case_id,
        "amount": amount,
        "pay_methods": {
            # æ–¹æ¡ˆA: å›ºå®šæ”¶æ¬¾ç  + å¤‡æ³¨ï¼ˆå…è´¹æ–¹æ¡ˆï¼‰
            "qr_code_url": "static/qr_codes/platform_wechat.jpg",
            "payment_note": f"æ¡ˆä»¶{case_id}è¿˜æ¬¾{amount}å…ƒ",
            # æ–¹æ¡ˆB: èšåˆæ”¯ä»˜ï¼ˆå°é¢ä»˜è´¹ï¼‰
            "payment_link": f"https://pay.workbridge.com/order/{order_id}",
            # æ–¹æ¡ˆC: é“¶è¡Œè½¬è´¦
            "bank_account": "å¹³å°ä¸“ç”¨æ”¶æ¬¾è´¦æˆ·ï¼š6228480088888888888",
            "bank_note": f"æ¡ˆä»¶{case_id}"
        }
    }
    
    # å‘é€ç»™å€ºåŠ¡äººçš„æ”¶æ¬¾ä¿¡æ¯
    send_payment_notice(debtor_info, order)
    
    return order
```

#### **1.2 åˆ°è´¦ç¡®è®¤æœºåˆ¶**
```python

    ç¡®è®¤æ”¶æ¬¾åˆ°è´¦ - æ”¯æŒå¤šç§ç¡®è®¤æ–¹å¼

        # é“¶è¡Œæµæ°´æ ¸å¯¹ï¼ˆéœ€è¦äººå·¥ï¼‰
        "bank_statement": {
            "reliability": "100%", 
            "time_delay": "24å°æ—¶",
            "cost": "äººå·¥æˆæœ¬"
        },
        # å€ºåŠ¡äººä¸»åŠ¨ä¸Šä¼ å‡­è¯
        "debtor_receipt": {
            "reliability": "95%",
            "time_delay": "äººå·¥å®¡æ ¸",
            "cost": "å…è´¹"
        }
    }
    
    # æ”¶æ¬¾ç¡®è®¤åç«‹å³è§¦å‘åˆ†è´¦
    if confirm_payment(payment_info):
        trigger_auto_split(payment_info)
```

### **Phase 2: æ™ºèƒ½åˆ†è´¦ç¯èŠ‚**

#### **2.1 åˆ†è´¦è§„åˆ™å¼•æ“**
```python
# åˆ†è´¦è§„åˆ™ - çµæ´»é…ç½®ï¼Œæ”¯æŒä¸ªæ€§åŒ–
class SplitRulesEngine:
    def __init__(self):
        # æ³¨æ„ï¼šè¿™é‡Œçš„æ¯”ä¾‹å®šä¹‰äº†å„æ–¹åœ¨"æœåŠ¡åˆ†æˆæ± "ä¸­çš„å æ¯”
        self.default_rates_in_pool = {
            "lawyer_rate": 0.20,         # å¾‹å¸ˆåˆ†æˆ20% (å æœåŠ¡æ± ) -> å¯¹åº”æ€»é‡‘é¢çš„10%
            "sales_rate": 0.15,          # é”€å”®åˆ†æˆ15% (å æœåŠ¡æ± ) -> å¯¹åº”æ€»é‡‘é¢çš„7.5%
            "platform_rate": 0.65        # å¹³å°åˆ†æˆ65% (å æœåŠ¡æ± ) -> å¯¹åº”æ€»é‡‘é¢çš„32.5%
        }
        self.institution_return_rate = 0.50 # æœºæ„å›ºå®šè¿”è¿˜50%
    
    def calculate_split(self, case_id, total_amount):
        """
        è®¡ç®—åˆ†è´¦é‡‘é¢ - æ”¯æŒç‰¹æ®Šæ¡æ¬¾
        """
        case_info = get_case_info(case_id)
        
        # 1. é¦–å…ˆåˆ†ç¦»æœºæ„è¿”è¿˜éƒ¨åˆ†å’ŒæœåŠ¡åˆ†æˆæ± 
        institution_amount = total_amount * self.institution_return_rate
        service_pool_amount = total_amount * (1 - self.institution_return_rate)

        # 2. åœ¨æœåŠ¡åˆ†æˆæ± å†…éƒ¨åˆ†é…
        lawyer_amount = service_pool_amount * self.default_rates_in_pool["lawyer_rate"]
        sales_amount = service_pool_amount * self.default_rates_in_pool["sales_rate"]
        platform_amount = service_pool_amount * self.default_rates_in_pool["platform_rate"]

        # æœ€ç»ˆåˆ†è´¦ç»“æœ
        splits = {
            "institution_amount": institution_amount,
            "lawyer_amount": lawyer_amount,
            "sales_amount": sales_amount,
            "platform_amount": platform_amount
        }
        
        # ç‰¹æ®Šæƒ…å†µè°ƒæ•´ (åŸºäºæœåŠ¡åˆ†æˆæ± è¿›è¡Œè°ƒæ•´)
        if case_info.get("high_difficulty"):
            # é«˜éš¾åº¦æ¡ˆä»¶ï¼Œå¾‹å¸ˆåˆ†æˆå¢åŠ 2%ï¼Œå¹³å°å‡å°‘2% (åŸºäºæœåŠ¡æ± )
            adjustment = service_pool_amount * 0.02
            splits["lawyer_amount"] += adjustment
            splits["platform_amount"] -= adjustment
        
        if case_info.get("large_client"):
            # å¤§å®¢æˆ·ï¼Œé”€å”®åˆ†æˆå¢åŠ 1%ï¼Œå¹³å°å‡å°‘1% (åŸºäºæœåŠ¡æ± )
            adjustment = service_pool_amount * 0.01
            splits["sales_amount"] += adjustment
            splits["platform_amount"] -= adjustment
        
        # ç¡®ä¿æ€»é¢ä¸€è‡´ï¼ˆé‡è¦ï¼ï¼‰
        total_split = sum(splits.values())
        if abs(total_split - total_amount) > 0.01:
            # å·®é¢å½’å…¥å¹³å°ï¼ˆé¿å…åˆ†è´¦é”™è¯¯ï¼‰
            splits["platform_amount"] += (total_amount - total_split)
        
        return splits
```

#### **2.2 è‡ªåŠ¨åˆ†è´¦æ‰§è¡Œ**
```python
# åˆ†è´¦æ‰§è¡Œ - æŠ€æœ¯å®ç°è¦ç®€å•å¯é 
def execute_auto_split(payment_record_id):
    """
    æ‰§è¡Œè‡ªåŠ¨åˆ†è´¦ - é‡ç‚¹æ˜¯èµ„é‡‘å®‰å…¨
    """
    payment = get_payment_record(payment_record_id)
    splits = calculate_split(payment.case_id, payment.amount)
    
    # åˆ›å»ºåˆ†è´¦è®°å½•ï¼ˆå…ˆè®°å½•ï¼Œåæ‰§è¡Œï¼‰
    split_record = create_split_record(payment, splits)
    
    try:
        # æ‰§è¡Œåˆ†è´¦è½¬è´¦
        results = []
        
        # 1. æœºæ„åˆ†è´¦ï¼ˆæœ€å¤§å¤´ï¼‰
        institution_result = transfer_to_institution(
            amount=splits["institution_amount"],
            account=get_institution_account(payment.case_id)
        )
        results.append(("institution", institution_result))
        
        # 2. å¾‹å¸ˆåˆ†è´¦
        lawyer_result = transfer_to_lawyer(
            amount=splits["lawyer_amount"],
            account=get_lawyer_account(payment.case_id)
        )
        results.append(("lawyer", lawyer_result))
        
        # 3. é”€å”®åˆ†è´¦
        sales_result = transfer_to_sales(
            amount=splits["sales_amount"],
            account=get_sales_account(payment.case_id)
        )
        results.append(("sales", sales_result))
        
        # 4. å¹³å°ç•™å­˜ï¼ˆæœ€åï¼Œç¡®ä¿èµ„é‡‘å®‰å…¨ï¼‰
        platform_result = {"status": "retained", "amount": splits["platform_amount"]}
        results.append(("platform", platform_result))
        
        # æ›´æ–°åˆ†è´¦çŠ¶æ€
        update_split_status(split_record.id, "completed", results)
        
        # å‘é€åˆ†è´¦é€šçŸ¥
        notify_split_completion(payment.case_id, splits)
        
    except Exception as e:
        # åˆ†è´¦å¤±è´¥å¤„ç† - å…³é”®æ˜¯èµ„é‡‘ä¸ä¸¢å¤±
        update_split_status(split_record.id, "failed", str(e))
        trigger_manual_review(split_record.id)
        send_alert_to_admin(f"åˆ†è´¦å¤±è´¥ï¼š{payment_record_id}, é”™è¯¯ï¼š{str(e)}")
```

### **Phase 3: å¯¹è´¦æ ¸å®ç¯èŠ‚**

#### **3.1 å®æ—¶å¯¹è´¦ç³»ç»Ÿ**
```python
# å¯¹è´¦ç³»ç»Ÿ - ç¡®ä¿èµ„é‡‘å‡†ç¡®
def daily_reconciliation():
    """
    æ¯æ—¥è‡ªåŠ¨å¯¹è´¦ - é˜²æ­¢èµ„é‡‘é”™è¯¯
    """
    today = datetime.now().date()
    
    # å¯¹è´¦å†…å®¹
    reconciliation = {
        "total_received": get_daily_received(today),      # æ€»æ”¶æ¬¾
        "total_distributed": get_daily_distributed(today), # æ€»åˆ†è´¦
        "platform_balance": get_platform_balance(),       # å¹³å°ä½™é¢
        "pending_splits": get_pending_splits(today),      # å¾…åˆ†è´¦
        "failed_splits": get_failed_splits(today)         # å¤±è´¥åˆ†è´¦
    }
    
    # æ ¸ç®—æ£€æŸ¥
    expected_balance = (
        reconciliation["total_received"] - 
        reconciliation["total_distributed"] - 
        reconciliation["pending_splits"]
    )
    
    actual_balance = reconciliation["platform_balance"]
    
    if abs(expected_balance - actual_balance) > 1.0:  # è¯¯å·®è¶…è¿‡1å…ƒ
        send_reconciliation_alert({
            "date": today,
            "expected": expected_balance,
            "actual": actual_balance,
            "difference": actual_balance - expected_balance
        })
    
    # ç”Ÿæˆå¯¹è´¦æŠ¥å‘Š
    generate_reconciliation_report(today, reconciliation)
```

#### **3.2 å¯¹è´¦æŠ¥å‘Šç”Ÿæˆ**
```python
# å¯¹è´¦æŠ¥å‘Š - ç»™å„æ–¹æŸ¥çœ‹
def generate_participant_statements(month):
    """
    ç”Ÿæˆå‚ä¸æ–¹æœˆåº¦å¯¹è´¦å•
    """
    # æœºæ„å¯¹è´¦å•
    for institution in get_all_institutions():
        statement = {
            "institution_name": institution.company_name,
            "period": month,
            "cases_processed": get_monthly_cases(institution.id, month),
            "total_recovery": get_monthly_recovery(institution.id, month),
            "institution_share": get_monthly_share(institution.id, month),
            "fee_breakdown": {
                "recovery_commission": "50%",
                "payment_processing_fee": "0.6%",
                "platform_service_fee": "0%"  # æˆ‘ä»¬ä¸æ”¶æœåŠ¡è´¹
            }
        }
        send_monthly_statement(institution, statement)
    
    # å¾‹å¸ˆå¯¹è´¦å•
    for lawyer in get_all_lawyers():
        statement = {
            "lawyer_name": lawyer.real_name,
            "period": month, 
            "cases_completed": get_monthly_completed_cases(lawyer.id, month),
            "success_rate": get_monthly_success_rate(lawyer.id, month),
            "total_commission": get_monthly_commission(lawyer.id, month),
            "performance_bonus": get_performance_bonus(lawyer.id, month)
        }
        send_monthly_statement(lawyer, statement)
```

### **Phase 4: ç»“ç®—æç°ç¯èŠ‚**

#### **4.1 æç°ç”³è¯·å¤„ç†**
```python
# æç°å¤„ç† - ç®€åŒ–ç”¨æˆ·æ“ä½œ
def process_withdrawal_request(user_id, user_type, amount):
    """
    å¤„ç†æç°ç”³è¯· - ç”¨æˆ·ä½“éªŒè¦å¥½
    """
    # éªŒè¯æç°æ¡ä»¶
    validation = validate_withdrawal(user_id, user_type, amount)
    if not validation["valid"]:
        return {"status": "rejected", "reason": validation["reason"]}
    
    # åˆ›å»ºæç°è®¢å•
    withdrawal = {
        "withdrawal_id": f"WD{int(time.time())}",
        "user_id": user_id,
        "user_type": user_type,
        "amount": amount,
        "fee": calculate_withdrawal_fee(amount),  # æç°æ‰‹ç»­è´¹
        "actual_amount": amount - calculate_withdrawal_fee(amount),
        "bank_info": get_user_bank_info(user_id),
        "status": "pending"
    }
    
    save_withdrawal_request(withdrawal)
    
    # è‡ªåŠ¨å¤„ç†ï¼ˆå°é¢ï¼‰æˆ–äººå·¥å®¡æ ¸ï¼ˆå¤§é¢ï¼‰
    if amount <= 10000:  # å°é¢è‡ªåŠ¨å¤„ç†
        process_auto_withdrawal(withdrawal)
    else:  # å¤§é¢äººå·¥å®¡æ ¸
        queue_manual_review(withdrawal)
    
    return {"status": "processing", "withdrawal_id": withdrawal["withdrawal_id"]}

def calculate_withdrawal_fee(amount):
    """æç°æ‰‹ç»­è´¹è®¡ç®—"""
    if amount <= 1000:
        return 2.0   # å°é¢å›ºå®š2å…ƒ
    elif amount <= 10000:
        return amount * 0.005  # 0.5%
    else:
        return min(amount * 0.003, 50)  # 0.3%ï¼Œæœ€é«˜50å…ƒ
```

### **å…³é”®æŠ€æœ¯å®ç°è¦ç‚¹**

- **ç”¨æˆ·æ»¡æ„åº¦**ï¼šç›®æ ‡4.5/5åˆ†+

### æŠ€æœ¯æŒ‡æ ‡
- **ç³»ç»Ÿå¯ç”¨æ€§**ï¼š99.9%+
- **å“åº”æ—¶é—´**ï¼š<200ms
- **Gasè´¹ä¼˜åŒ–**ï¼šèŠ‚çœ50%+

### è´¢åŠ¡æŒ‡æ ‡å’Œæ”¶å…¥é¢„æµ‹ï¼ˆçµæ´»ç”¨å·¥é«˜åˆ©æ¶¦æ¨¡å¼ï¼‰
#### **ç¬¬ä¸€å¹´æ”¶å…¥ç›®æ ‡**
- **å‚¬æ”¶ä¸šåŠ¡ä¸»è¥**ï¼šå¤„ç†10äº¿å‚¬æ”¶é‡‘é¢
  - æœºæ„è¿”è¿˜ï¼š5äº¿ (50%)
  - æœåŠ¡åˆ†æˆæ± ï¼š5äº¿ (50%)
    - å¹³å°åˆ†æˆï¼š3.25äº¿ (æœåŠ¡æ± çš„65%)
    - å¾‹å¸ˆä½£é‡‘ï¼š1äº¿ (æœåŠ¡æ± çš„20%)
    - é”€å”®ä½£é‡‘ï¼š7500ä¸‡ (æœåŠ¡æ± çš„15%)
- **SaaSè®¢é˜…è´¹**ï¼š200å®¶æœºæ„Ã—Â¥3999/æœˆÃ—12æœˆ=960ä¸‡
- **å¢å€¼æœåŠ¡è´¹**ï¼šAIæ–‡æ¡£ã€ä¸“ä¸šåˆ†æç­‰=500ä¸‡
- **å¹³å°æ€»è¥æ”¶**ï¼š3.25äº¿ + 960ä¸‡ + 500ä¸‡ = **3.396äº¿**

#### **è¿è¥æˆæœ¬æ§åˆ¶ï¼ˆè½»èµ„äº§æ¨¡å¼ï¼‰**
- **æŠ€æœ¯å›¢é˜Ÿ**ï¼š800ä¸‡ï¼ˆ10äººæ ¸å¿ƒå›¢é˜Ÿï¼‰
- **å¸‚åœºæ¨å¹¿**ï¼š500ä¸‡ï¼ˆè·å®¢æˆæœ¬Â¥2500/æœºæ„ï¼‰
- **è¿è¥æ”¯æŒ**ï¼š300ä¸‡ï¼ˆå®¢æœã€æ³•åŠ¡ã€è´¢åŠ¡ï¼‰
- **åŠå…¬ç§Ÿèµ**ï¼š100ä¸‡
- **æ€»æˆæœ¬é¢„ç®—**ï¼š1700ä¸‡
- **å‡€åˆ©æ¶¦**ï¼š3.396äº¿ - 1700ä¸‡ = **3.226äº¿**
- **å‡€åˆ©æ¶¦ç‡**ï¼š95%

#### **å…³é”®è´¢åŠ¡æ¯”ç‡ï¼ˆçªå‡ºä¼˜åŠ¿ï¼‰**
- **æ¯›åˆ©ç‡**ï¼š95%

#### **å‘ç¥¨è‡ªåŠ¨åŒ–å¤„ç†æµç¨‹**
```python
class InvoiceAutomationSystem:
    def __init__(self):
        self.invoice_templates = {
            "platform_service": "æŠ€æœ¯æœåŠ¡è´¹å‘ç¥¨æ¨¡æ¿",
            "lawyer_service": "æ³•å¾‹æœåŠ¡è´¹å‘ç¥¨æ¨¡æ¿",
            "business_service": "å‚¬æ”¶æœåŠ¡è´¹å‘ç¥¨æ¨¡æ¿"
        }
        self.tax_rates = {
            "platform_tech_service": 0.06,    # æŠ€æœ¯æœåŠ¡6%å¢å€¼ç¨
            "lawyer_service": 0.06,           # æ³•å¾‹æœåŠ¡6%å¢å€¼ç¨  
            "collection_service": 0.06        # å‚¬æ”¶æœåŠ¡6%å¢å€¼ç¨
        }
    
    def process_automatic_invoicing(self, payment_record):
        """
        æ”¶æ¬¾åè‡ªåŠ¨è§¦å‘å‘ç¥¨å¼€å…·æµç¨‹
        """
        settlement_data = self.get_settlement_data(payment_record.case_id)
        invoice_requests = []
        
        # 1. å¹³å°æŠ€æœ¯æœåŠ¡è´¹å‘ç¥¨ï¼ˆå¹³å°å¼€å…·ç»™æœºæ„ï¼‰
        platform_invoice = {
            "issuer": "WorkBridgeå¹³å°",
            "recipient": settlement_data["institution_info"],
            "amount": settlement_data["platform_amount"],
            "tax_amount": settlement_data["platform_amount"] * self.tax_rates["platform_tech_service"],
            "description": f"æ¡ˆä»¶{payment_record.case_id}æŠ€æœ¯æœåŠ¡è´¹",
            "invoice_type": "å¢å€¼ç¨ä¸“ç”¨å‘ç¥¨",
            "auto_send": True,
            "cost_deduction": "ä»æœºæ„åˆ†æˆä¸­æ‰£é™¤ç¨è´¹"
        }
        invoice_requests.append(platform_invoice)
        
        # 2. å¾‹å¸ˆæœåŠ¡è´¹å‘ç¥¨ï¼ˆå¾‹å¸ˆå¼€å…·ç»™æœºæ„ï¼‰
        lawyer_invoice = {
            "issuer": settlement_data["lawyer_info"]["tax_entity"],
            "recipient": settlement_data["institution_info"],
            "amount": settlement_data["lawyer_amount"],
            "tax_amount": settlement_data["lawyer_amount"] * self.tax_rates["lawyer_service"],
            "description": f"æ¡ˆä»¶{payment_record.case_id}æ³•å¾‹æœåŠ¡è´¹",
            "invoice_type": "å¢å€¼ç¨ä¸“ç”¨å‘ç¥¨",
            "auto_send": True,
            "cost_deduction": "ä»å¾‹å¸ˆä½£é‡‘ä¸­æ‰£é™¤ç¨è´¹"
        }
        invoice_requests.append(lawyer_invoice)
        
        # 3. å‚¬æ”¶æœåŠ¡è´¹å‘ç¥¨ï¼ˆæœºæ„å¼€å…·ç»™å€ºåŠ¡äººï¼‰
        collection_invoice = {
            "issuer": settlement_data["institution_info"],
            "recipient": settlement_data["debtor_info"],
            "amount": payment_record.amount,
            "tax_amount": payment_record.amount * self.tax_rates["collection_service"],
            "description": f"æ¡ˆä»¶{payment_record.case_id}å€ºåŠ¡å‚¬æ”¶æœåŠ¡è´¹",
            "invoice_type": "å¢å€¼ç¨æ™®é€šå‘ç¥¨",
            "auto_send": True,
            "cost_bearer": "æœºæ„æ‰¿æ‹…å¼€ç¥¨æˆæœ¬"
        }
        invoice_requests.append(collection_invoice)
        
        # 4. å‘ç¥¨æˆæœ¬ä»å¯¹åº”æ–¹æ”¶å…¥ä¸­æ‰£é™¤
        self.deduct_invoice_costs(settlement_data, invoice_requests)
        
        # 5. è‡ªåŠ¨å‘é€å‘ç¥¨å¼€å…·è¯·æ±‚
        return self.batch_send_invoice_requests(invoice_requests)
    
    def deduct_invoice_costs(self, settlement_data, invoice_requests):
        """
        å‘ç¥¨æˆæœ¬è‡ªåŠ¨æ‰£é™¤ - ç¡®ä¿å¹³å°é›¶æˆæœ¬
        """
        cost_deductions = {
            "institution": 0,
            "lawyer": 0,
            "platform": 0
        }
        
        for invoice in invoice_requests:
            if invoice["issuer"] == "WorkBridgeå¹³å°":
                # å¹³å°å¼€ç¥¨æˆæœ¬ä»æœºæ„åˆ†æˆæ‰£é™¤
                cost_deductions["institution"] += invoice["tax_amount"] + 50  # å¼€ç¥¨æ‰‹ç»­è´¹50å…ƒ
            elif "å¾‹å¸ˆ" in invoice["issuer"]:
                # å¾‹å¸ˆå¼€ç¥¨æˆæœ¬ä»å¾‹å¸ˆä½£é‡‘æ‰£é™¤
                cost_deductions["lawyer"] += invoice["tax_amount"] + 30   # å¼€ç¥¨æ‰‹ç»­è´¹30å…ƒ
            elif invoice["issuer"] == settlement_data["institution_info"]["name"]:
                # æœºæ„å¼€ç¥¨æˆæœ¬æœºæ„è‡ªå·±æ‰¿æ‹…
                cost_deductions["institution"] += invoice["tax_amount"] + 30
        
        # æ›´æ–°å®é™…åˆ°è´¦é‡‘é¢
        self.update_final_settlement_amounts(settlement_data["case_id"], cost_deductions)
        
        return cost_deductions
```

### **åˆ†æœŸè¿˜æ¬¾é£é™©æ§åˆ¶æœºåˆ¶**

    "risk_sharing_model": {
        "platform_protection": "15%å®‰å…¨è¾¹é™…è¦†ç›–åè´¦é£é™©",
        "insurance_coverage": "ä¸ä¿é™©å…¬å¸åˆä½œï¼Œä¿éšœå¤§é¢åè´¦",

            "10-30%": "åˆ†æˆå‡å°‘50%",

        },
        "final_closure": {

#### **åè´¦å¤„ç†è‡ªåŠ¨åŒ–ç³»ç»Ÿ**
```python
class InstallmentRiskManager:
    def __init__(self):
        self.risk_thresholds = {
            "high_risk": 0.3,      # é€¾æœŸ30%è§¦å‘é«˜é£é™©
            "critical_risk": 0.6,   # é€¾æœŸ60%è§¦å‘å…³é”®é£é™©  
            "write_off": 0.9       # é€¾æœŸ90%è¿›å…¥æ ¸é”€æµç¨‹
        }
        self.insurance_threshold = 100000  # 10ä¸‡ä»¥ä¸Šæ¡ˆä»¶å¿…é¡»æŠ•ä¿
    
    def monitor_installment_progress(self, case_id):
        """
        åˆ†æœŸè¿›åº¦ç›‘æ§ - å®æ—¶é£é™©è¯„ä¼°
        """
        case_data = self.get_case_data(case_id)
        payment_history = self.get_payment_history(case_id)
        
        # è®¡ç®—å®Œæˆç‡å’Œé€¾æœŸç‡
        completion_rate = payment_history["completed_amount"] / case_data["total_amount"]
        overdue_rate = payment_history["overdue_amount"] / case_data["total_amount"]
        
        # é£é™©ç­‰çº§è¯„ä¼°
        if overdue_rate >= self.risk_thresholds["write_off"]:
            return self.initiate_write_off_process(case_id)
        elif overdue_rate >= self.risk_thresholds["critical_risk"]:
            return self.escalate_collection_efforts(case_id)
        elif overdue_rate >= self.risk_thresholds["high_risk"]:
            return self.activate_insurance_claim(case_id)
        else:
            return {"status": "normal", "action": "continue_monitoring"}
    
    def handle_partial_completion(self, case_id, final_completion_rate):
        """
        éƒ¨åˆ†å®Œæˆå¤„ç† - åŠ¨æ€è°ƒæ•´åˆ†æˆ
        """
        if final_completion_rate >= 0.6:
            # æ­£å¸¸åˆ†æˆ
            return self.execute_normal_settlement(case_id)
        elif final_completion_rate >= 0.3:
            # åˆ†æˆå‡å°‘20%
            return self.execute_reduced_settlement(case_id, penalty_rate=0.2)
        elif final_completion_rate >= 0.1:
            # åˆ†æˆå‡å°‘50%
            return self.execute_reduced_settlement(case_id, penalty_rate=0.5)
        else:
            # ä»…æ”¯ä»˜åŸºç¡€æˆæœ¬ï¼Œè¿½å›å·²ä»˜ä½£é‡‘
            return self.execute_cost_recovery(case_id)
    
    def insurance_integration(self, case_id, case_amount):
        """
        ä¿é™©ç†èµ”é›†æˆ - å¤§é¢æ¡ˆä»¶é£é™©è½¬ç§»
        """
        if case_amount >= self.insurance_threshold:
            insurance_request = {
                "case_id": case_id,
                "insured_amount": case_amount * 0.8,  # æ‰¿ä¿80%
                "premium_rate": 0.02,                 # ä¿è´¹2%
                "premium_payer": "institution",       # æœºæ„æ”¯ä»˜ä¿è´¹
                "claim_trigger": "completion_rate < 30%",
                "coverage_period": "12_months"
            }
            
            return self.submit_insurance_application(insurance_request)
        else:
            # å°é¢æ¡ˆä»¶å¹³å°å®‰å…¨è¾¹é™…è¦†ç›–
            return {"status": "platform_coverage", "coverage": "safety_margin"}
```

### **æ›´å¤šé€‚åˆçš„ä¸šåŠ¡åœºæ™¯æ‰©å±•**

            "market_size": "8000äº¿åŒ»ç–—æœåŠ¡å¸‚åœº",

#### **åœºæ™¯æ‰©å±•ç­–ç•¥**
```python
class ScenarioExpansionStrategy:
    def __init__(self):
        self.expansion_priority = [
            "åœ¨çº¿æ•™è‚²åŸ¹è®­",    # ä¼˜å…ˆçº§1ï¼šAIä¼˜åŒ–ç©ºé—´æœ€å¤§
            "æˆ¿åœ°äº§ä¸­ä»‹",      # ä¼˜å…ˆçº§2ï¼šå®¢å•ä»·æœ€é«˜  
            "åŒ»ç–—å¥åº·å’¨è¯¢",    # ä¼˜å…ˆçº§3ï¼šåˆšéœ€+é«˜é¢‘
            "ä¼ä¸šå’¨è¯¢æœåŠ¡",    # ä¼˜å…ˆçº§4ï¼šå¤åˆ¶æ€§å¼º
            "Web3æŠ€æœ¯å¼€å‘"     # ä¼˜å…ˆçº§5ï¼šæœªæ¥è¶‹åŠ¿
        ]
    
    def evaluate_scenario_fit(self, scenario_name):
        """
        åœºæ™¯é€‚é…åº¦è¯„ä¼° - ç¡®å®šæ˜¯å¦é€‚åˆå¹³å°æ¨¡å¼
        """
        scenario = SUITABLE_BUSINESS_SCENARIOS["high_compatibility_scenarios"][scenario_name]
        
        fit_score = 0
        
        # å¤šæ–¹å‚ä¸è¯„åˆ†ï¼ˆ30åˆ†ï¼‰
        if len(scenario["participants"]) >= 4:
            fit_score += 30
        elif len(scenario["participants"]) == 3:
            fit_score += 20
        
        # AIä¼˜åŒ–æ½œåŠ›è¯„åˆ†ï¼ˆ25åˆ†ï¼‰
        ai_keywords = ["AIç”Ÿæˆ", "æ™ºèƒ½", "è‡ªåŠ¨", "ç®—æ³•"]
        ai_mentions = sum(1 for keyword in ai_keywords if keyword in scenario["ai_optimization"])
        fit_score += min(ai_mentions * 5, 25)
        
        # å¸‚åœºè§„æ¨¡è¯„åˆ†ï¼ˆ25åˆ†ï¼‰
        market_size_str = scenario["market_size"]
        if "ä¸‡äº¿" in market_size_str:
            fit_score += 25
        elif "åƒäº¿" in market_size_str or "5000äº¿" in market_size_str:
            fit_score += 20
        elif "1000äº¿" in market_size_str:
            fit_score += 15
        
        # å•†ä¸šæ¨¡å¼åŒ¹é…åº¦ï¼ˆ20åˆ†ï¼‰
        if "æ‰˜ç®¡" in scenario["payment_flow"] and "è‡ªåŠ¨åˆ†è´¦" in scenario["payment_flow"]:
            fit_score += 20
        
        return {
            "scenario": scenario_name,
            "fit_score": fit_score,
            "recommendation": "é«˜åº¦æ¨è" if fit_score >= 80 else "é€‚åº¦æ¨è" if fit_score >= 60 else "è°¨æ…è€ƒè™‘",
            "expansion_timeline": "6ä¸ªæœˆå†…" if fit_score >= 80 else "12ä¸ªæœˆå†…" if fit_score >= 60 else "å¾…è¯„ä¼°"
        }
```

**è¿™ä¸ªé€šç”¨çµæ´»ç”¨å·¥SaaSå¹³å°ï¼Œé€šè¿‡AIä¼˜åŒ–ä¼ ç»Ÿä¸šåŠ¡æµç¨‹+å¾®ä¿¡ç”Ÿæ€æ·±åº¦èåˆ+åŒæ¨¡å¼è¿è¥+é€šç”¨åŒ–é…ç½®çš„å››é‡åˆ›æ–°ï¼Œæ„å»ºäº†ä¸€ä¸ªå…·å¤‡æŒ‡æ•°çº§å¢é•¿æ½œåŠ›çš„å•†ä¸šç”Ÿæ€ç³»ç»Ÿï¼**

## ğŸš€ **ä¸šåŠ¡ç³»ç»Ÿåˆå§‹åŒ–æµç¨‹è®¾è®¡**

### **å¾‹å¸ˆèº«ä»½éªŒè¯ä¸èµ„è´¨è®¤è¯ç³»ç»Ÿ**

#### **æ ¸å¿ƒéªŒè¯æµç¨‹ï¼ˆä¸‰é‡éªŒè¯æœºåˆ¶ï¼‰**
```python
# å¾‹å¸ˆèº«ä»½éªŒè¯å®Œæ•´æµç¨‹
class LawyerVerificationSystem:
    def __init__(self):
        self.verification_stages = ["åŸºç¡€éªŒè¯", "èµ„è´¨è®¤è¯", "å®æ“è€ƒæ ¸"]
        self.pass_threshold = 85  # ç»¼åˆè¯„åˆ†85åˆ†ä»¥ä¸Šé€šè¿‡
    
    def stage_1_basic_verification(self, lawyer_application):
        """
        ç¬¬ä¸€é˜¶æ®µï¼šåŸºç¡€èº«ä»½éªŒè¯ï¼ˆå¿…é¡»é¡¹ï¼‰
        """
        verification_tasks = {
            # 1. æ‰§ä¸šè¯ä¹¦OCRè¯†åˆ«+å®˜æ–¹éªŒè¯
            "license_verification": {
                "ocr_recognition": self.ocr_scan_license(lawyer_application.license_image),
                "official_check": self.query_justice_bureau_database(lawyer_application.license_no),
                "validity_check": self.check_license_validity(lawyer_application.license_no),
                "weight": 40,
                "required": True
            },
            
            # 2. èº«ä»½è¯å®åè®¤è¯
            "identity_verification": {
                "id_card_ocr": self.ocr_scan_id_card(lawyer_application.id_image),
                "face_recognition": self.face_compare_verification(lawyer_application.face_image),
                "public_security_check": self.verify_real_name(lawyer_application.id_number),
                "weight": 30,
                "required": True
            },
            
            # 3. æ‰§ä¸šå¾‹æ‰€éªŒè¯
            "law_firm_verification": {
                "firm_registration": self.verify_law_firm_registration(lawyer_application.firm_name),
                "employment_proof": self.verify_employment_relationship(lawyer_application),
                "firm_authorization": self.check_firm_authorization_letter(lawyer_application),
                "weight": 20,
                "required": True
            },
            
            # 4. è”ç³»æ–¹å¼éªŒè¯
            "contact_verification": {
                "phone_verification": self.verify_phone_number(lawyer_application.phone),
                "email_verification": self.verify_email_address(lawyer_application.email),
                "wechat_binding": self.bind_wechat_account(lawyer_application.wechat_id),
                "weight": 10,
                "required": True
            }
        }
        
        # æ‰§è¡ŒéªŒè¯å¹¶æ‰“åˆ†
        verification_result = self.execute_verification_tasks(verification_tasks)
        
        if verification_result["total_score"] >= 90:
            return {"stage_1_result": "passed", "proceed_to_stage_2": True}
        else:
            return {"stage_1_result": "failed", "rejection_reason": verification_result["failed_items"]}
    
    def stage_2_professional_certification(self, lawyer_id):
        """
        ç¬¬äºŒé˜¶æ®µï¼šä¸“ä¸šèµ„è´¨è®¤è¯ï¼ˆèƒ½åŠ›è¯„ä¼°ï¼‰
        """
        certification_tests = {
            # 1. æ³•å¾‹ä¸“ä¸šçŸ¥è¯†è€ƒè¯•ï¼ˆAIå‡ºé¢˜ï¼‰
            "legal_knowledge_test": {
                "debt_collection_law": self.generate_ai_test_questions("å‚¬æ”¶ç›¸å…³æ³•å¾‹", 20),
                "contract_law": self.generate_ai_test_questions("åˆåŒæ³•", 15),
                "civil_procedure": self.generate_ai_test_questions("æ°‘äº‹è¯‰è®¼ç¨‹åº", 10),
                "score_weight": 40,
                "pass_score": 80
            },
            
            # 2. å®é™…æ¡ˆä¾‹åˆ†æ
            "case_analysis": {
                "case_scenarios": self.provide_mock_debt_cases(5),
                "solution_evaluation": self.ai_evaluate_solutions,
                "time_limit": 120,  # 120åˆ†é’Ÿ
                "score_weight": 35,
                "pass_score": 75
            },
            
            # 3. å‚¬æ”¶è¯æœ¯ä¸æ²Ÿé€šæŠ€å·§
            "communication_skills": {
                "role_play_scenarios": self.create_debtor_communication_scenarios(3),
                "response_evaluation": self.evaluate_communication_approach,
                "compliance_check": self.check_legal_compliance,
                "score_weight": 25,
                "pass_score": 70
            }
        }
        
        certification_result = self.execute_certification_tests(certification_tests)
        
        # æ ¹æ®æµ‹è¯•ç»“æœåˆ†é…ä¸“ä¸šç­‰çº§
        if certification_result["total_score"] >= 90:
            return {"professional_level": "é«˜çº§å¾‹å¸ˆ", "commission_rate": 0.38, "case_limit": 15}
        elif certification_result["total_score"] >= 80:
            return {"professional_level": "ä¸­çº§å¾‹å¸ˆ", "commission_rate": 0.35, "case_limit": 10}
        else:
            return {"professional_level": "åˆçº§å¾‹å¸ˆ", "commission_rate": 0.32, "case_limit": 5}
    
    def stage_3_operational_assessment(self, lawyer_id):
        """
        ç¬¬ä¸‰é˜¶æ®µï¼šå®æ“è€ƒæ ¸ï¼ˆè¯•ç”¨æœŸè¯„ä¼°ï¼‰
        """
        trial_period_config = {
            "trial_duration": 30,  # 30å¤©è¯•ç”¨æœŸ
            "trial_cases": 3,      # è¯•ç”¨æœŸå¤„ç†3ä¸ªæ¡ˆä»¶
            "supervision_level": "å¯†åˆ‡ç›‘ç£",
            "evaluation_criteria": {
                "success_rate": {"target": 60, "weight": 40},
                "compliance_score": {"target": 95, "weight": 30},
                "client_satisfaction": {"target": 80, "weight": 20},
                "response_speed": {"target": 24, "weight": 10}  # 24å°æ—¶å†…å“åº”
            }
        }
        
        return self.start_trial_period(lawyer_id, trial_period_config)
```

#### **å¾‹å¸ˆèµ„è´¨åŠ¨æ€ç®¡ç†**
```python
# å¾‹å¸ˆèµ„è´¨æŒç»­ç›‘æ§ä¸æ›´æ–°
class LawyerQualificationManager:
    def __init__(self):
        self.monitoring_frequency = "daily"
        self.auto_verification_apis = {
            "justice_bureau": "å¸æ³•éƒ¨å¾‹å¸ˆæŸ¥è¯¢API",
            "credit_system": "å¾‹å¸ˆä¿¡ç”¨ä¿¡æ¯ç³»ç»Ÿ",
            "disciplinary_records": "å¾‹å¸ˆæƒ©æˆ’ä¿¡æ¯åº“"
        }
    
    def continuous_qualification_monitoring(self, lawyer_id):
        """
        æŒç»­èµ„è´¨ç›‘æ§ - ç¡®ä¿å¾‹å¸ˆå§‹ç»ˆåˆè§„
        """
        monitoring_tasks = {
            # æ¯æ—¥æ‰§ä¸šè¯æœ‰æ•ˆæ€§æ£€æŸ¥
            "daily_license_check": {
                "license_status": self.check_license_status_daily(lawyer_id),
                "suspension_alerts": self.monitor_license_suspension(lawyer_id),
                "renewal_reminders": self.check_license_expiry(lawyer_id)
            },
            
            # æ¯å‘¨ä¿¡ç”¨è®°å½•æ£€æŸ¥
            "weekly_credit_check": {
                "disciplinary_records": self.check_new_disciplinary_actions(lawyer_id),
                "court_sanctions": self.monitor_court_sanctions(lawyer_id),
                "professional_complaints": self.check_client_complaints(lawyer_id)
            },
            
            # æ¯æœˆç»©æ•ˆè¯„ä¼°
            "monthly_performance_review": {
                "success_rate_trend": self.analyze_success_rate_trend(lawyer_id),
                "client_satisfaction_trend": self.analyze_satisfaction_trend(lawyer_id),
                "compliance_score_trend": self.analyze_compliance_trend(lawyer_id)
            }
        }
        
        # æ ¹æ®ç›‘æ§ç»“æœè‡ªåŠ¨è°ƒæ•´å¾‹å¸ˆç­‰çº§å’Œæƒé™
        return self.auto_adjust_lawyer_privileges(lawyer_id, monitoring_tasks)
    
    def lawyer_level_adjustment(self, lawyer_id, performance_data):
        """
        æ ¹æ®è¡¨ç°åŠ¨æ€è°ƒæ•´å¾‹å¸ˆç­‰çº§
        """
        current_level = get_lawyer_current_level(lawyer_id)
        
        # å‡çº§æ¡ä»¶æ£€æŸ¥
        if performance_data["monthly_success_rate"] > 85 and performance_data["client_satisfaction"] > 90:
            new_level = self.promote_lawyer_level(lawyer_id)
            self.increase_commission_rate(lawyer_id, 0.02)  # æå‡2%ä½£é‡‘
            self.increase_case_limit(lawyer_id, 5)          # å¢åŠ 5ä¸ªæ¡ˆä»¶é¢åº¦
        
        # é™çº§é£é™©æ£€æŸ¥
        elif performance_data["monthly_success_rate"] < 40 or performance_data["compliance_score"] < 70:
            self.initiate_improvement_plan(lawyer_id)
            self.reduce_case_limit(lawyer_id, 3)            # å‡å°‘3ä¸ªæ¡ˆä»¶é¢åº¦
            
        # ä¸¥é‡è¿è§„å¤„ç†
        if performance_data["compliance_violations"] > 0:
            self.suspend_lawyer_temporarily(lawyer_id)
            self.initiate_compliance_review(lawyer_id)
```

# å€ºåŠ¡äººä¿¡æ¯æ‰¹é‡å¯¼å…¥ç³»ç»Ÿ
class DebtorDataImportSystem:
    def __init__(self):
        self.supported_formats = ["Excel", "CSV", "JSON", "XML", "æ•°æ®åº“ç›´è¿"]
        self.max_batch_size = 10000  # å•æ¬¡æœ€å¤šå¯¼å…¥1ä¸‡æ¡è®°å½•
        self.validation_rules = self.load_validation_rules()
    
    def batch_import_debtor_data(self, import_request):
        """
        æ‰¹é‡å¯¼å…¥å€ºåŠ¡äººä¿¡æ¯ - æ”¯æŒå¤šç§æ•°æ®æº
        """
        import_process = {
            # 1. æ•°æ®æºæ¥å…¥ä¸æ ¼å¼è½¬æ¢
            "data_ingestion": {
                "file_upload": self.handle_file_upload(import_request.file_path),
                "database_connection": self.connect_institution_database(import_request.db_config),
                "api_integration": self.integrate_institution_api(import_request.api_config),
                "format_standardization": self.standardize_data_format()
            },
            
            # 2. æ•°æ®æ¸…æ´—ä¸éªŒè¯
            "data_validation": {
                "required_fields_check": self.validate_required_fields(),
                "data_format_validation": self.validate_data_formats(),
                "duplicate_detection": self.detect_duplicate_records(),
                "data_quality_scoring": self.calculate_data_quality_score()
            },
            
            # 3. æ•°æ®å¢å¼ºä¸é£é™©è¯„ä¼°
            "data_enhancement": {
                "phone_location_lookup": self.lookup_phone_locations(),
                "name_validity_check": self.validate_name_authenticity(),
                "debt_risk_assessment": self.assess_collection_difficulty(),
                "priority_scoring": self.calculate_collection_priority()
            },
            
            # 4. æ‰¹é‡å…¥åº“ä¸åˆ†é…
            "data_processing": {
                "batch_database_insert": self.batch_insert_debtor_records(),
                "case_auto_generation": self.auto_generate_collection_cases(),
                "lawyer_auto_assignment": self.auto_assign_to_lawyers(),
                "notification_sending": self.send_import_completion_notice()
            }
        }
        
        return self.execute_import_process(import_process)
    
    def validate_debtor_data_quality(self, debtor_record):
        """
        å€ºåŠ¡äººæ•°æ®è´¨é‡éªŒè¯ - ç¡®ä¿æ•°æ®å¯ç”¨æ€§
        """
        validation_checklist = {
            # å¿…å¡«å­—æ®µéªŒè¯
            "required_fields": {
                "debtor_name": {"status": "required", "pattern": r"^[\u4e00-\u9fa5]{2,10}$"},
                "id_number": {"status": "required", "pattern": r"^\d{17}[\dXx]$"},
                "phone_number": {"status": "required", "pattern": r"^1[3-9]\d{9}$"},
                "debt_amount": {"status": "required", "min": 1000, "max": 10000000},
                "overdue_days": {"status": "required", "min": 1, "max": 3650}
            },
            
            # æ•°æ®ä¸€è‡´æ€§éªŒè¯
            "consistency_check": {
                "id_name_match": self.verify_id_name_consistency(debtor_record),
                "phone_region_match": self.verify_phone_region_consistency(debtor_record),
                "debt_amount_reasonableness": self.check_debt_amount_reasonableness(debtor_record)
            },
            
            # ä¸šåŠ¡é€»è¾‘éªŒè¯
            "business_logic": {
                "duplicate_check": self.check_existing_debtor(debtor_record),
                "institution_authorization": self.verify_institution_authorization(debtor_record),
                "legal_collection_feasibility": self.assess_legal_feasibility(debtor_record)
            }
        }
        
        validation_result = self.execute_validation(validation_checklist, debtor_record)
        
        # æ•°æ®è´¨é‡è¯„åˆ†ï¼ˆ100åˆ†åˆ¶ï¼‰
        quality_score = self.calculate_quality_score(validation_result)
        
        if quality_score >= 90:
            return {"status": "excellent", "auto_assign": True, "priority": "high"}
        elif quality_score >= 70:
            return {"status": "good", "auto_assign": True, "priority": "medium"}
        elif quality_score >= 50:
            return {"status": "acceptable", "auto_assign": False, "manual_review": True}
        else:
            return {"status": "poor", "reject": True, "reasons": validation_result["errors"]}
```

#### **ä¸šåŠ¡æ± ç®¡ç†ä¸è´¨é‡è¯„ä¼°ç³»ç»Ÿ**
```python
# ä¸šåŠ¡æ± ç®¡ç†ç³»ç»Ÿ - ç¡®ä¿ä¸šåŠ¡è´¨é‡å’Œå¯è¿½æº¯æ€§
class BusinessPoolManager:
    def __init__(self):
        self.quality_score_range = (0, 100)
        self.minimum_quality_threshold = 70
        self.business_lifecycle_tracking = True
    
    def business_injection_process(self, business_batch, sales_id):
        """
        ä¸šåŠ¡æ³¨å…¥æµç¨‹ - ä»ä¸Šä¼ åˆ°ç¡®è®¤çš„å®Œæ•´é“¾è·¯
        """
        injection_pipeline = {
            # 1. ä¸šåŠ¡æ•°æ®ä¸Šä¼ ä¸éªŒè¯
            "upload_validation": {
                "data_format_check": self.validate_business_data_format(business_batch),
                "completeness_verification": self.check_data_completeness(business_batch),
                "duplicate_detection": self.detect_duplicate_businesses(business_batch),
                "legal_compliance_check": self.verify_legal_compliance(business_batch)
            },
            
            # 2. ä¸šåŠ¡è´¨é‡é¢„è¯„ä¼°
            "preliminary_assessment": {
                "debt_amount_reasonableness": self.assess_debt_amounts(business_batch),
                "debtor_contact_validity": self.validate_contact_information(business_batch),
                "collection_feasibility": self.evaluate_collection_probability(business_batch),
                "business_source_credibility": self.verify_business_source(sales_id)
            },
            
            # 3. ä¸šåŠ¡æ± æ­£å¼æ³¨å…¥
            "pool_injection": {
                "business_id_generation": self.generate_unique_business_ids(business_batch),
                "sales_attribution_binding": self.bind_sales_attribution(business_batch, sales_id),
                "priority_ranking": self.calculate_business_priority(business_batch),
                "lawyer_assignment_queue": self.add_to_assignment_queue(business_batch)
            },
            
            # 4. è´¨é‡ç›‘æ§å¯åŠ¨
            "quality_monitoring_setup": {
                "baseline_quality_score": self.calculate_initial_quality_score(business_batch),
                "performance_tracking_initiation": self.setup_performance_tracking(business_batch),
                "milestone_checkpoints": self.define_quality_checkpoints(business_batch),
                "feedback_collection_mechanism": self.setup_feedback_collection(business_batch)
            }
        }
        
        injection_result = self.execute_injection_pipeline(injection_pipeline)
        
        # ä¸šåŠ¡æ³¨å…¥æˆåŠŸé€šçŸ¥
        self.notify_injection_success(sales_id, injection_result)
        
        return injection_result
    
    def business_quality_evaluation_system(self, business_id):
        """
        ä¸šåŠ¡è´¨é‡ç»¼åˆè¯„ä¼° - å¤šç»´åº¦è´¨é‡è¯„åˆ†
        """
        evaluation_dimensions = {
            # æ•°æ®è´¨é‡ç»´åº¦ï¼ˆ30%æƒé‡ï¼‰
            "data_quality": {
                "completeness": self.evaluate_data_completeness(business_id),
                "accuracy": self.evaluate_data_accuracy(business_id),
                "consistency": self.evaluate_data_consistency(business_id),
                "timeliness": self.evaluate_data_timeliness(business_id),
                "weight": 0.30
            },
            
            # æ‰§è¡Œæ•ˆæœç»´åº¦ï¼ˆ40%æƒé‡ï¼‰
            "execution_effectiveness": {
                "success_rate": self.calculate_collection_success_rate(business_id),
                "timeline_adherence": self.evaluate_timeline_performance(business_id),
                "client_satisfaction": self.measure_client_satisfaction(business_id),
                "legal_compliance": self.assess_compliance_performance(business_id),
                "weight": 0.40
            },
            
            # ä¸šåŠ¡ä»·å€¼ç»´åº¦ï¼ˆ20%æƒé‡ï¼‰  
            "business_value": {
                "recovery_amount": self.calculate_recovery_value(business_id),
                "cost_efficiency": self.evaluate_cost_effectiveness(business_id),
                "roi_performance": self.calculate_business_roi(business_id),
                "repeat_business_potential": self.assess_repeat_potential(business_id),
                "weight": 0.20
            },
            
            # åˆä½œè´¨é‡ç»´åº¦ï¼ˆ10%æƒé‡ï¼‰
            "cooperation_quality": {
                "communication_responsiveness": self.evaluate_communication_quality(business_id),
                "problem_resolution_speed": self.assess_problem_handling(business_id),
                "additional_support_provision": self.evaluate_support_quality(business_id),
                "feedback_incorporation": self.assess_feedback_responsiveness(business_id),
                "weight": 0.10
            }
        }
        
        # ç»¼åˆè´¨é‡è¯„åˆ†è®¡ç®—
        total_quality_score = self.calculate_weighted_quality_score(evaluation_dimensions)
        
        # è´¨é‡ç­‰çº§åˆ’åˆ†
        quality_grade = self.determine_quality_grade(total_quality_score)
        
        # æ”¹è¿›å»ºè®®ç”Ÿæˆ
        improvement_suggestions = self.generate_improvement_suggestions(evaluation_dimensions)
        
        return {
            "business_id": business_id,
            "quality_score": total_quality_score,
            "quality_grade": quality_grade,
            "dimension_scores": evaluation_dimensions,
            "improvement_suggestions": improvement_suggestions,
            "evaluation_timestamp": datetime.now(),
            "next_evaluation_due": datetime.now() + timedelta(days=30)
        }
    
    def sales_performance_comprehensive_tracking(self, sales_id):
        """
        é”€å”®ä¸šç»©ç»¼åˆè·Ÿè¸ª - å…³è”ä¸šåŠ¡è´¨é‡å’Œæœ€ç»ˆæ•ˆæœ
        """
        performance_analytics = {
            # ä¸šåŠ¡è´¡çŒ®åˆ†æ
            "business_contribution": {
                "total_businesses_uploaded": self.count_uploaded_businesses(sales_id),
                "successful_injections": self.count_successful_injections(sales_id),
                "injection_success_rate": self.calculate_injection_success_rate(sales_id),
                "average_business_quality": self.calculate_average_quality_score(sales_id)
            },
            
            # æ‰§è¡Œæ•ˆæœè·Ÿè¸ª
            "execution_results": {
                "total_recovery_amount": self.sum_recovery_amounts(sales_id),
                "average_collection_success_rate": self.calculate_avg_success_rate(sales_id),
                "client_retention_rate": self.calculate_client_retention(sales_id),
                "business_completion_timeline": self.analyze_completion_timelines(sales_id)
            },
            
            # æ”¶ç›Šåˆ†æˆè®°å½•
            "commission_tracking": {
                "total_commission_earned": self.calculate_total_commission(sales_id),
                "monthly_commission_trend": self.analyze_commission_trend(sales_id),
                "commission_per_business": self.calculate_avg_commission_per_business(sales_id),
                "performance_bonus_earned": self.calculate_performance_bonuses(sales_id)
            },
            
            # è´¨é‡æ”¹è¿›è¶‹åŠ¿
            "quality_improvement": {
                "quality_score_trend": self.analyze_quality_trend(sales_id),
                "problem_resolution_improvement": self.track_problem_resolution(sales_id),
                "client_feedback_improvement": self.track_feedback_improvements(sales_id),
                "repeat_business_generation": self.track_repeat_business(sales_id)
            }
        }
        
        # ç»¼åˆè¡¨ç°è¯„çº§
        overall_rating = self.calculate_sales_overall_rating(performance_analytics)
        
        # æœªæ¥åˆä½œå»ºè®®
        cooperation_recommendations = self.generate_cooperation_recommendations(performance_analytics)
        
        return {
            "sales_id": sales_id,
            "performance_analytics": performance_analytics,
            "overall_rating": overall_rating,
            "cooperation_recommendations": cooperation_recommendations,
            "evaluation_period": self.get_evaluation_period(),
            "next_review_date": self.calculate_next_review_date()
        }
```

## ğŸ› ï¸ **åå°åˆ†æˆæ¯”ä¾‹é…ç½®ç³»ç»Ÿ**

### **åŠ¨æ€é…ç½®ç®¡ç†**
```python
# åå°åˆ†æˆæ¯”ä¾‹é…ç½®ç³»ç»Ÿ
class CommissionConfigurationSystem:
    def __init__(self):
        self.config_table = "commission_configurations"
        self.default_splits = {
            "institution_return": 0.50,     # æœºæ„50%ï¼ˆè¿”è¿˜å§”æ‰˜æ–¹ï¼‰
            "service_pool": 0.50,           # æœåŠ¡åˆ†æˆæ± 50%
            "lawyer_rate_in_pool": 0.20,    # å¾‹å¸ˆå æœåŠ¡æ± 20%ï¼ˆæ€»å›æ¬¾10%ï¼‰
            "sales_rate_in_pool": 0.15,     # é”€å”®å æœåŠ¡æ± 15%ï¼ˆæ€»å›æ¬¾7.5%ï¼‰
            "platform_rate_in_pool": 0.65   # å¹³å°å æœåŠ¡æ± 65%ï¼ˆæ€»å›æ¬¾32.5%ï¼‰
        }
        
    def update_commission_rates(self, tenant_id, new_rates, updated_by):
        """
        æ›´æ–°åˆ†æˆæ¯”ä¾‹é…ç½® - æ”¯æŒå®æ—¶è°ƒæ•´
        """
        # éªŒè¯æ€»æ¯”ä¾‹ç­‰äº100%
        total_rate = sum(new_rates.values())
        if abs(total_rate - 1.0) > 0.001:
            raise ValueError(f"æ€»åˆ†æˆæ¯”ä¾‹å¿…é¡»ç­‰äº100%ï¼Œå½“å‰ï¼š{total_rate*100:.1f}%")
        
        # éªŒè¯è¿è¥æˆæœ¬è¦†ç›–
        if new_rates.get("platform_rate", 0) < 0.25:
            raise ValueError("å¹³å°åˆ†æˆä¸èƒ½ä½äº25%ï¼Œæ— æ³•è¦†ç›–å‘ç¥¨ã€äººå‘˜ã€æˆ¿ç§Ÿç­‰è¿è¥æˆæœ¬")
        
        # ä¿å­˜å†å²é…ç½®
        self.backup_current_config(tenant_id, updated_by)
        
        # æ›´æ–°é…ç½®
        config_update = {
            "tenant_id": tenant_id,
            "institution_rate": new_rates.get("institution_rate", self.default_splits["institution_rate"]),
            "platform_rate": new_rates.get("platform_rate", self.default_splits["platform_rate"]),
            "lawyer_rate": new_rates.get("lawyer_rate", self.default_splits["lawyer_rate"]),
            "sales_rate": new_rates.get("sales_rate", self.default_splits["sales_rate"]),
            "updated_by": updated_by,
            "updated_at": datetime.now(),
            "effective_from": datetime.now() + timedelta(hours=1),  # 1å°æ—¶åç”Ÿæ•ˆ
            "change_reason": new_rates.get("change_reason", "")
        }
        
        # ä¿å­˜æ–°é…ç½®
        self.save_commission_config(config_update)
        
        # å‘é€å˜æ›´é€šçŸ¥
        self.notify_commission_change(tenant_id, config_update)
        
        return {
            "status": "success",
            "message": "åˆ†æˆæ¯”ä¾‹é…ç½®å·²æ›´æ–°ï¼Œ1å°æ—¶åç”Ÿæ•ˆ",
            "new_config": config_update,
            "cost_analysis": self.analyze_cost_impact(config_update)
        }
    
    def analyze_cost_impact(self, config):
        """
        åˆ†æé…ç½®å˜æ›´å¯¹è¿è¥æˆæœ¬çš„å½±å“
        """
        monthly_costs = {
            "invoice_processing": 50000,    # å‘ç¥¨å¤„ç†äººå‘˜
            "office_rent": 120000,          # åŠå…¬å®¤ç§Ÿé‡‘
            "utilities": 30000,             # æ°´ç”µè´¹
            "ai_infrastructure": 200000,    # AIç³»ç»Ÿç»´æŠ¤
            "legal_compliance": 80000,      # æ³•åŠ¡åˆè§„
            "marketing": 150000,            # å¸‚åœºæ¨å¹¿
            "customer_service": 100000      # å®¢æœæ”¯æŒ
        }
        
        total_monthly_cost = sum(monthly_costs.values())
        platform_revenue_needed = total_monthly_cost / config["platform_rate"]
        
        return {
            "monthly_operating_cost": total_monthly_cost,
            "platform_rate": f"{config['platform_rate']*100:.1f}%",
            "min_monthly_revenue_needed": platform_revenue_needed,
            "cost_coverage_status": "âœ… å……è¶³" if config["platform_rate"] >= 0.25 else "âš ï¸ ä¸è¶³"
        }
```

            </div>
            
            <div class="cost-impact">
                <h4>è¿è¥æˆæœ¬å½±å“åˆ†æ</h4>
                <div id="cost-analysis" class="cost-display">
                    <p>æœˆåº¦è¿è¥æˆæœ¬: Â¥730,000</p>
                    <p>æ‰€éœ€æœ€ä½æ”¶å…¥: Â¥<span id="min-revenue">2,085,714</span></p>
                    <p>æˆæœ¬è¦†ç›–çŠ¶æ€: <span id="coverage-status" class="status-ok">âœ… å……è¶³</span></p>
                </div>
            </div>
            
            <button type="submit" id="submit-config" class="btn-primary">
                æ›´æ–°é…ç½®ï¼ˆ1å°æ—¶åç”Ÿæ•ˆï¼‰
            </button>
        </form>
    </div>

<script>
// å®æ—¶é…ç½®éªŒè¯å’Œæˆæœ¬åˆ†æ
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
    const inputs = ['institution-rate', 'platform-rate', 'lawyer-rate', 'sales-rate'];
    const monthlyCost = 730000; // æœˆåº¦è¿è¥æˆæœ¬
    
    function validateAndUpdate() {
        let total = 0;
        const rates = {};
        
        inputs.forEach(id => {
            const value = parseFloat(document.getElementById(id).value) || 0;
            rates[id.replace('-rate', '')] = value;
            total += value;
        });
        
        // æ›´æ–°æ€»è®¡æ˜¾ç¤º
        const totalDisplay = document.getElementById('new-total-rate');
        const statusDisplay = document.getElementById('total-status');
        const warningsDisplay = document.getElementById('validation-warnings');
        
        totalDisplay.textContent = total.toFixed(1) + '%';
        
        // éªŒè¯é€»è¾‘
        const warnings = [];
        let isValid = true;
        
        if (Math.abs(total - 100) > 0.1) {
            warnings.push('æ€»æ¯”ä¾‹å¿…é¡»ç­‰äº100%');
            isValid = false;
        }
        
        if (rates.platform < 25) {
            warnings.push('å¹³å°åˆ†æˆä¸èƒ½ä½äº25%ï¼ˆè¿è¥æˆæœ¬è¦æ±‚ï¼‰');
            isValid = false;
        }
        
        // æ›´æ–°çŠ¶æ€æ˜¾ç¤º
        if (isValid) {
            statusDisplay.textContent = 'âœ…';
            statusDisplay.className = 'status-ok';
            document.getElementById('submit-config').disabled = false;
        } else {
            statusDisplay.textContent = 'âŒ';
            statusDisplay.className = 'status-error';
            document.getElementById('submit-config').disabled = true;
        }
        
        // æ˜¾ç¤ºè­¦å‘Š
        warningsDisplay.innerHTML = warnings.map(w => `<p class="warning">âš ï¸ ${w}</p>`).join('');
        
        // æˆæœ¬åˆ†æ
        const minRevenue = monthlyCost / (rates.platform / 100);
        document.getElementById('min-revenue').textContent = minRevenue.toLocaleString();
        
        const coverageStatus = document.getElementById('coverage-status');
        if (rates.platform >= 25) {
            coverageStatus.textContent = 'âœ… å……è¶³';
            coverageStatus.className = 'status-ok';
        } else {
            coverageStatus.textContent = 'âš ï¸ ä¸è¶³';
            coverageStatus.className = 'status-warning';
        }
    }
    
    // ç»‘å®šäº‹ä»¶ç›‘å¬
    inputs.forEach(id => {
        document.getElementById(id).addEventListener('input', validateAndUpdate);
    });
    
    // åˆå§‹åŒ–
    validateAndUpdate();
});
</script>
```

---

## ğŸ¢ **æ‰©å±•çµæ´»ç”¨å·¥åœºæ™¯è¯¦ç»†è®¾è®¡**

### **1. æˆ¿åœ°äº§ä¸­ä»‹åœºæ™¯**

#### **ä¸šåŠ¡æ¨¡å¼é…ç½®**

## ğŸŒŸ **åœºæ™¯æ‰©å±•æˆ˜ç•¥æ€»ç»“**

### **ç»Ÿä¸€å¹³å°ä»·å€¼ä¸»å¼ **

æ— è®ºåœ¨å“ªä¸ªåœºæ™¯ï¼ŒWorkBridgeéƒ½æä¾›ï¼š

### **åˆ†æˆæ¯”ä¾‹ä¼˜åŒ–è¯´æ˜**

è°ƒæ•´åçš„åˆ†æˆç»“æ„ï¼ˆæœºæ„50% + å¹³å°35% + å¾‹å¸ˆ25% + é”€å”®15% = 100%ï¼‰æ›´å¥½åœ°åæ˜ äº†ï¼š

- **å¹³å°ä»·å€¼**ï¼š35%åˆ†æˆæ”¯æ’‘AIç³»ç»Ÿå¼€å‘ã€è¿è¥æˆæœ¬ï¼ˆå‘ç¥¨ã€äººå‘˜ã€æˆ¿ç§Ÿã€æ°´ç”µç­‰ï¼‰
- **è¿è¥ä¿éšœ**ï¼šå……è¶³çš„å¹³å°æ”¶ç›Šç¡®ä¿æœåŠ¡è´¨é‡å’ŒæŒç»­åˆ›æ–°
- **åˆç†æ¿€åŠ±**ï¼šå¾‹å¸ˆ25%ã€é”€å”®15%ä¿æŒè¶³å¤Ÿå¸å¼•åŠ›
- **æˆæœ¬è¦†ç›–**ï¼šæœˆåº¦73ä¸‡è¿è¥æˆæœ¬å¾—åˆ°æœ‰æ•ˆè¦†ç›–

**é€šè¿‡åå°çµæ´»é…ç½®ç³»ç»Ÿå’Œå¤šåœºæ™¯æ‰©å±•èƒ½åŠ›ï¼ŒWorkBridgeå°†æˆä¸ºçœŸæ­£çš„é€šç”¨çµæ´»ç”¨å·¥SaaSå¹³å°ï¼Œä¸€å¥—æŠ€æœ¯æ¶æ„æœåŠ¡å¤šä¸ªå‚ç›´è¡Œä¸šï¼Œå®ç°è§„æ¨¡åŒ–ç›ˆåˆ©ï¼** ğŸš€ğŸ’

### 5. å‰ç«¯ç•Œé¢å·®å¼‚åŒ–æ˜¾ç¤ºä¸æ•°æ®éš”ç¦»

ä¸ºå¢å¼ºç”¨æˆ·æ¿€åŠ±å¹¶ä¿æŠ¤å¹³å°å•†ä¸šæœºå¯†ï¼Œç³»ç»Ÿå°†å¯¹ä¸åŒè§’è‰²å±•ç¤ºå·®å¼‚åŒ–çš„åˆ†æˆä¿¡æ¯ã€‚

- **æ ¸å¿ƒåŸåˆ™**ï¼šå¾‹å¸ˆå’Œé”€å”®äººå‘˜çš„æ‰€æœ‰ç•Œé¢ï¼ˆä¸ªäººä¸­å¿ƒã€ä¸šç»©ç»Ÿè®¡ã€ç»“ç®—å•ï¼‰å‡åŸºäº"**æœåŠ¡åˆ†æˆæ± **"é‡‘é¢ï¼ˆå³æœºæ„è¿”è¿˜åçš„å‰©ä½™éƒ¨åˆ†ï¼‰è¿›è¡Œè®¡ç®—å’Œå±•ç¤ºï¼Œå¯¹ä»–ä»¬éšè—"æ€»å›æ¬¾é‡‘é¢"çš„æ¦‚å¿µã€‚

```javascript

    // å¾‹å¸ˆè§†å›¾
    lawyer_view: {
        commission_rate: "20%",  // æ˜¾ç¤ºç›¸å¯¹äº"æœåŠ¡åˆ†æˆæ± "çš„æ¯”ä¾‹
        rate_description: "æ‚¨å°†è·å¾—æœåŠ¡åˆ†æˆæ± çš„20%ä½œä¸ºä½£é‡‘",

        // ç®¡ç†å‘˜å¯ä»¥çœ‹åˆ°æ‰€æœ‰å±‚çº§çš„æ•°æ®

- **å…³é”®ç‚¹**ï¼š
  - **å¯¹ä¸šåŠ¡äººå‘˜ä¸å¯è§**ï¼šå¹³å°çš„35%åˆ†æˆã€æœºæ„çš„50%è¿”è¿˜å¯¹å¾‹å¸ˆå’Œé”€å”®å®Œå…¨é€æ˜ã€‚
  - **å¼ºåŒ–æ„ŸçŸ¥**ï¼š"20%"å’Œ"15%"åœ¨è§†è§‰ä¸Šæ¯”"10%"å’Œ"7.5%"æ›´å…·å¸å¼•åŠ›ï¼Œç¬¦åˆ"å·æ¢æ¦‚å¿µ"çš„è¥é”€ç­–ç•¥ã€‚
  - **é€»è¾‘é—­ç¯**ï¼šä¸ªäººåå°çš„ä¸šç»©ç»Ÿè®¡ã€æ”¶å…¥è®¡ç®—å™¨ç­‰æ‰€æœ‰æ¨¡å—ï¼Œå‡ä»¥æ­¤å£å¾„ä¸ºå‡†ï¼Œå½¢æˆé€»è¾‘è‡ªæ´½ã€‚
```

### **æ•°æ®å¯è§æ€§ä¸å±•ç¤ºé€»è¾‘ (æ ¸å¿ƒè®¾è®¡)**

ä¸ºå®ç°å¯¹å¤–æ¿€åŠ±ä¸å¯¹å†…æˆæœ¬æ§åˆ¶çš„å¹³è¡¡ï¼Œç³»ç»Ÿé‡‡ç”¨åŒå±‚æ•°æ®å±•ç¤ºé€»è¾‘ã€‚æ­¤è®¾è®¡ä¸ºå¹³å°æ ¸å¿ƒå•†ä¸šç­–ç•¥ï¼Œå¼€å‘æ—¶å¿…é¡»ä¸¥æ ¼éµå®ˆã€‚

**1. ä¸¤å¤§æ ¸å¿ƒé‡‘é¢æ¦‚å¿µå®šä¹‰**

- **æ€»å›æ¬¾é‡‘é¢ (Total Collected Amount)**: å€ºåŠ¡äººå®é™…æ”¯ä»˜çš„å…¨éƒ¨æ¬¾é¡¹ï¼Œæ˜¯æ‰€æœ‰è®¡ç®—çš„æœ€é«˜å±‚çº§çš„åŸºæ•°ã€‚**æ­¤æ•°æ®ä»…å¯¹å¹³å°ç®¡ç†å‘˜å¯è§**ã€‚
- **æœåŠ¡åˆ†æˆæ±  (Service Pool)**: æ€»å›æ¬¾é‡‘é¢æ‰£é™¤è¿”è¿˜ç»™é‡‘èæœºæ„çš„50%åï¼Œå‰©ä½™çš„å¯ä¾›å¹³å°ã€å¾‹å¸ˆã€é”€å”®ä¸‰æ–¹åˆ†é…çš„é‡‘é¢ã€‚è®¡ç®—å…¬å¼ä¸ºï¼š`æœåŠ¡åˆ†æˆæ±  = æ€»å›æ¬¾é‡‘é¢ * 50%`ã€‚

**2. è§’è‰²æ•°æ®è®¿é—®æƒé™**

- **å¾‹å¸ˆ (Lawyer) & é”€å”® (Sales)**:
    - **ç»å¯¹éš”ç¦»**: åœ¨ä»–ä»¬çš„æ‰€æœ‰ç•Œé¢ï¼ŒåŒ…æ‹¬ä¸ªäººä¸­å¿ƒã€ä»ªè¡¨æ¿ã€ä¸šç»©æŠ¥è¡¨ã€ç»“ç®—å•ç­‰ï¼Œ**ç»å¯¹ä¸èƒ½**å‡ºç°"æ€»å›æ¬¾é‡‘é¢"ã€‚
    - **å”¯ä¸€åŸºæ•°**: æ‰€æœ‰ä¸ä»–ä»¬ç›¸å…³çš„"æ€»é‡‘é¢"ã€"ä¸šç»©åŸºæ•°"ç­‰ï¼Œ**å¿…é¡»**æ˜¯"æœåŠ¡åˆ†æˆæ± "çš„é‡‘é¢ã€‚
    - **å±•ç¤ºæ¯”ä¾‹**: ä»–ä»¬çœ‹åˆ°çš„ä½£é‡‘æ¯”ä¾‹æ˜¯åŸºäº"æœåŠ¡åˆ†æˆæ± "è®¡ç®—çš„ï¼ˆå¾‹å¸ˆ20%ï¼Œé”€å”®15%ï¼‰ã€‚

- **å¹³å°ç®¡ç†å‘˜ (Admin)**:
    - **å®Œå…¨å¯è§**: æ‹¥æœ‰æœ€é«˜æƒé™ï¼Œå¯ä»¥çœ‹åˆ°ä»"æ€»å›æ¬¾é‡‘é¢"åˆ°å„æ–¹æœ€ç»ˆåˆ†æˆçš„å®Œæ•´èµ„é‡‘é“¾è·¯å’ŒçœŸå®æ•°æ®ã€‚

**3. åç«¯å®ç°ä¼ªä»£ç ç¤ºä¾‹**

```python
# æ•°æ®æŸ¥è¯¢å±‚çš„æƒé™æ§åˆ¶
def get_performance_data(user_id, role):
    """
    æ ¹æ®ç”¨æˆ·è§’è‰²è¿”å›ä¸åŒçš„ä¸šç»©æ•°æ®è§†å›¾
    """
    if role in ['lawyer', 'sales']:
        # å¯¹äºå¾‹å¸ˆå’Œé”€å”®ï¼Œä»"æœåŠ¡åˆ†æˆæ± "è§†å›¾ä¸­æŸ¥è¯¢æ•°æ®
        # SQLæŸ¥è¯¢ç¤ºä¾‹: SELECT ... FROM V_SERVICE_POOL_PERFORMANCE WHERE user_id = ...
        data = query_from_service_pool_view(user_id)
        
        # è¿”å›çš„æ•°æ®ä¸åŒ…å«æ€»å›æ¬¾é¢
        # ä¾‹å¦‚: data['total_base_amount'] æ˜¯æœåŠ¡åˆ†æˆæ± çš„é‡‘é¢
        return {
            "display_commission_rate": "20%" if role == 'lawyer' else "15%",
            "performance_base_amount": data.service_pool_total, # ä¸šç»©åŸºæ•°æ˜¯æœåŠ¡æ± é‡‘é¢
            "calculated_commission": data.commission_amount
        }
        
    elif role == 'admin':
        # ç®¡ç†å‘˜ä»åŒ…å«æ‰€æœ‰çœŸå®æ•°æ®çš„è§†å›¾ä¸­æŸ¥è¯¢
        # SQLæŸ¥è¯¢ç¤ºä¾‹: SELECT ... FROM V_FULL_FINANCIALS WHERE ...
        data = query_from_full_financial_view()
        
        return {
            "total_collected_amount": data.total_collected,
            "institution_return": data.institution_amount,
            "service_pool_amount": data.service_pool,
            "platform_share": data.platform_amount,
            "lawyer_share": data.lawyer_amount,
            "sales_share": data.sales_amount
        }
    else:
        raise PermissionError("æ— æƒè®¿é—®æ•°æ®")

```
**4. æ€»ç»“**

æ­¤è®¾è®¡æ˜¯æ•´ä¸ªå•†ä¸šæ¨¡å¼èƒ½å¤ŸæˆåŠŸçš„å…³é”®ã€‚å®ƒé€šè¿‡"ä¿¡æ¯å·®"å’Œ"æ¦‚å¿µåŒ…è£…"ï¼Œåœ¨ä¸ç‰ºç‰²å¹³å°åˆ©æ¶¦çš„å‰æä¸‹ï¼Œæå¤§åœ°æå‡äº†å¯¹å¾‹å¸ˆå’Œé”€å”®çš„å¸å¼•åŠ›ï¼Œæ˜¯å¹³å°çš„æ ¸å¿ƒç«äº‰åŠ›ä¹‹ä¸€ã€‚

### **é€šç”¨åŒ–é…ç½®å¼•æ“**
```python
# ä¸šåŠ¡æµç¨‹é…ç½®å¼•æ“ - åå°å¯è§†åŒ–é…ç½®
class BusinessProcessConfigurator:
    def configure_workflow(self, tenant_id, scenario_type):
        """
        å¯è§†åŒ–é…ç½®ä¸šåŠ¡æµç¨‹ - æ‹–æ‹½å¼æµç¨‹è®¾è®¡
        """
        workflow_templates = {
            "legal_collection": [
                {"step": "case_assignment", "configurable": True},
                {"step": "document_generation", "ai_enabled": True},
                {"step": "communication_sequence", "multichannel": True},
                {"step": "payment_tracking", "split_rules": "configurable"},
                {"step": "completion_verification", "auto_manual": "both"}
            ],
            "web3_development": [
                {"step": "requirement_analysis", "ai_assisted": True},
                {"step": "developer_matching", "skill_based": True},
                {"step": "milestone_planning", "smart_contracts": True},
                {"step": "code_review", "automated": True},
                {"step": "payment_release", "escrow_based": True}
            ]
        }
        
        return self.customize_workflow(workflow_templates[scenario_type], tenant_id)
